  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## PREAMBLE\n'
  '\n'
  'WE, THE PEOPLE OF INDIA, having solemnly resolved to constitute\n'
  'India into a 1[SOVEREIGN SOCIALIST SECULAR DEMOCRATIC\n'
  'REPUBLIC] and to secure to all its citizens:\n'
  '\n'
  'JUSTICE, social, economic and political;\n'
  '\n'
  'LIBERTY of thought, expression, belief, faith and worship;\n'
  'EQUALITY of status and of opportunity;\n'
  '\n'
  'and to promote among them all\n'
  '\n'
  'FRATERNITY assuring the dignity of the individual and the 2[unity\n'
  'and integrity of the Nation];\n'
  '\n'
  'IN OUR CONSTITUENT ASSEMBLY this twenty-sixth day of\n'
  'November, 1949, do HEREBY ADOPT, ENACT AND GIVE TO\n'
  'OURSELVES THIS CONSTITUTION.\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Subs. by the Constitution (Forty-second Amendment) Act, 1976, s.2, for '
  '"SOVEREIGN\n'
  'DEMOCRATIC REPUBLIC" (w.e.f. 3-1-1977).\n'
  '\n'
  '2\\. Subs. by s. 2, ibid., for "Unity of the Nation" (w.e.f. 3-1-1977).\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## PART I THE UNION AND ITS TERRITORY\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Name and territory of the Union .- (1) India, that is Bharat,\n'
  'shall be a Union of States.\n'
  '\n'
  '1[(2) The States and the territories thereof shall be as specified in\n'
  'the First Schedule.]\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) The territory of India shall comprise\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) the territories of the States;\n'
  '\n'
  '2[(b) the Union territories specified in the First Schedule;\n'
  'and]\n'
  '\n'
  '(c) such other territories as may be acquired.\n'
  '\n'
  '2\\. Admission or establishment of new States .- Parliament may\n'
  'by law admit into the Union, or establish, new States on such terms and\n'
  'conditions as it thinks fit.\n'
  '\n'
  '3[2A. [Sikkim to be associated with the Union.] .- Omitted by the\n'
  'Constitution (Thirty-sixth Amendment) Act, 1975, s. 5 (w.e.f. 26-4-1975).]\n'
  '\n'
  '3\\. Formation of new States and alteration of areas,\n'
  'boundaries or names of existing States .- Parliament may by law-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) form a new State by separation of territory from any\n'
  'State or by uniting two or more States or parts of States or by\n'
  'uniting any territory to a part of any State;\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) increase the area of any State;\n'
  '\n'
  '(c) diminish the area of any State;\n'
  '\n'
  '(d) alter the boundaries of any State;\n'
  '\n'
  '(e) alter the name of any State:\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Subs. by the Constitution (Seventh Amendment) Act, 1956, s. 2, for cl. '
  '(2)\n'
  '(w.e.f. 1-11-1956).\n'
  '\n'
  '2\\. Subs. by s. 2 ibid. for sub-clause (b) (w.e.f. 1-11-1956).\n'
  '\n'
  '3\\. Ins. by the Constitution (Thirty-fifth Amendment) Act, 1974, s. 2 '
  '(w.e.f. 1-3-1975).\n'

  '## PART II CITIZENSHIP\n'
  '\n'
  '5\\. Citizenship at the commencement of the Constitution .- At the\n'
  'commencement of this Constitution, every person who has his domicile in '
  'the\n'
  'territory of India and-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) who was born in the territory of India; or\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) either of whose parents was born in the territory of India; or\n'
  '\n'
  '(c) who has been ordinarily resident in the territory of India for\n'
  'not less than five years immediately preceding such commencement,\n'
  'shall be a citizen of India.\n'
  '\n'
  '6\\. Rights of citizenship of certain persons who have migrated to\n'
  'India from Pakistan .- Notwithstanding anything in article 5, a person who\n'
  'has migrated to the territory of India from the territory now included in\n'
  'Pakistan shall be deemed to be a citizen of India at the commencement of '
  'this\n'
  'Constitution if-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) he or either of his parents or any of his grand-parents was born\n'
  'in India as defined in the Government of India Act, 1935 (as originally\n'
  'enacted); and\n'
  '\n'
  '(b)(i) in the case where such person has so migrated before the\n'
  'nineteenth day of July, 1948, he has been ordinarily resident in the\n'
  'territory of India since the date of his migration, or\n'
  '\n'
  '(ii) in the case where such person has so migrated on or after the\n'
  'nineteenth day of July, 1948, he has been registered as a citizen of India\n'
  'by an officer appointed in that behalf by the Government of the\n'
  'Dominion of India on an application made by him therefor to such\n'
  'officer before the commencement of this Constitution in the form and\n'
  'manner prescribed by that Government:\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that no person shall be so registered unless he has been resident\n'
  'in the territory of India for at least six months immediately preceding the '
  'date\n'
  'of his application.\n'
  '\n'
  '7\\. Rights of citizenship of certain migrants to Pakistan .-\n'
  'Notwithstanding anything in articles 5 and 6, a person who has after the '
  'first\n'
  'day of March, 1947, migrated from the territory of India to the territory '
  'now\n'
  'included in Pakistan shall not be deemed to be a citizen of India:\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="4" -->\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'

  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '### (Part II .- Citizenship)\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that nothing in this article shall apply to a person who, after\n'
  'having so migrated to the territory now included in Pakistan, has returned '
  'to the\n'
  'territory of India under a permit for resettlement or permanent return '
  'issued by\n'
  'or under the authority of any law and every such person shall for the '
  'purposes\n'
  'of clause (b) of article 6 be deemed to have migrated to the territory of '
  'India\n'
  'after the nineteenth day of July, 1948.\n'
  '\n'
  '8\\. Rights of citizenship of certain persons of Indian origin residing\n'
  'outside India .- Notwithstanding anything in article 5, any person who or\n'
  'either of whose parents or any of whose grand-parents was born in India as\n'
  'defined in the Government of India Act, 1935 (as originally enacted), and '
  'who\n'
  'is ordinarily residing in any country outside India as so defined shall be '
  'deemed\n'
  'to be a citizen of India if he has been registered as a citizen of India by '
  'the\n'
  'diplomatic or consular representative of India in the country where he is '
  'for the\n'
  'time being residing on an application made by him therefor to such '
  'diplomatic\n'
  'or consular representative, whether before or after the commencement of '
  'this\n'
  'Constitution, in the form and manner prescribed by the Government of the\n'
  'Dominion of India or the Government of India.\n'
  '\n'
  '9\\. Persons voluntarily acquiring citizenship of a foreign State not to\n'
  'be citizens .- No person shall be a citizen of India by virtue of article '
  '5, or be\n'
  'deemed to be a citizen of India by virtue of article 6 or article 8, if he '
  'has\n'
  'voluntarily acquired the citizenship of any foreign State.\n'
  '\n'
  '10\\. Continuance of the rights of citizenship .- Every person who is or\n'
  'is deemed to be a citizen of India under any of the foregoing provisions of '
  'this\n'
  'Part shall, subject to the provisions of any law that may be made by '
  'Parliament,\n'
  'continue to be such citizen.\n'
  '\n'
  '11\\. Parliament to regulate the right of citizenship by law .- Nothing\n'
  'in the foregoing provisions of this Part shall derogate from the power of\n'
  'Parliament to make any provision with respect to the acquisition and\n'
  'termination of citizenship and all other matters relating to citizenship.\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## PART III FUNDAMENTAL RIGHTS\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '### General\n'
  '\n'
  '12\\. Definition .- In this Part, unless the context otherwise requires, '
  '"the\n'
  'State" includes the Government and Parliament of India and the Government\n'
  'and the Legislature of each of the States and all local or other '
  'authorities within\n'
  'the territory of India or under the control of the Government of India.\n'
  '\n'
  '13\\. Laws inconsistent with or in derogation of the fundamental\n'
  'rights .- (1) All laws in force in the territory of India immediately '
  'before the\n'
  'commencement of this Constitution, in so far as they are inconsistent with '
  'the\n'
  'provisions of this Part, shall, to the extent of such inconsistency, be '
  'void.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) The State shall not make any law which takes away or abridges the\n'
  'rights conferred by this Part and any law made in contravention of this '
  'clause\n'
  'shall, to the extent of the contravention, be void.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) In this article, unless the context otherwise requires,-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) "law" includes any Ordinance, order, bye-law, rule, regulation,\n'
  'notification, custom or usage having in the territory of India the force '
  'of\n'

  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '### (Part III .- Fundamental Rights)\n'
  '\n'
  'Explanation .- For the purposes of this article and article 16,\n'
  '"economically weaker sections" shall be such as may be notified by the '
  'State\n'
  'from time to time on the basis of family income and other indicators of\n'
  'economic disadvantage.]\n'
  '\n'
  '16\\. Equality of opportunity in matters of public employment. (1)\n'
  'There shall be equality of opportunity for all citizens in matters relating '
  'to\n'
  'employment or appointment to any office under the State.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) No citizen shall, on grounds only of religion, race, caste, sex, '
  'descent,\n'
  'place of birth, residence or any of them, be ineligible for, or '
  'discriminated against\n'
  'in respect of, any employment or office under the State.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) Nothing in this article shall prevent Parliament from making any law\n'
  'prescribing, in regard to a class or classes of employment or appointment '
  'to an\n'
  'office "[under the Government of, or any local or other authority within, a '
  'State\n'
  'or Union territory, any requirement as to residence within that State or '
  'Union\n'
  'territory] prior to such employment or appointment.\n'
  '\n'
  '(4) Nothing in this article shall prevent the State from making any\n'
  'provision for the reservation of appointments or posts in favour of any\n'
  'backward class of citizens which, in the opinion of the State, is not '
  'adequately\n'
  'represented in the services under the State.\n'
  '\n'
  '2[(4A) Nothing in this article shall prevent the State from making any\n'
  'provision for reservation 3[in matters of promotion, with consequential\n'
  'seniority, to any class] or classes of posts in the services under the '
  'State in\n'
  'favour of the Scheduled Castes and the Scheduled Tribes which, in the '
  'opinion\n'
  'of the State, are not adequately represented in the services under the '
  'State.]\n'
  '\n'
  '4[(4B) Nothing in this article shall prevent the State from considering\n'
  'any unfilled vacancies of a year which are reserved for being filled up in '
  'that\n'
  'year in accordance with any provision for reservation made under clause (4) '
  'or\n'
  'clause (4A) as a separate class of vacancies to be filled up in any '
  'succeeding\n'
  'year or years and such class of vacancies shall not be considered together '
  'with\n'
  'the vacancies of the year in which they are being filled up for determining '
  'the\n'
  'ceiling of fifty per cent. reservation on total number of vacancies of that '
  'year.]\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Subs. by the Constitution (Seventh Amendment) Act, 1956, s. 29 and '
  'Sch., for "under\n'
  'any State specified in the First Schedule or any local or other authority '
  'within its\n'
  'territory, any requirement as to residence within that State" (w.e.f. '
  '1-11-1956).\n'
  '\n'
  '2\\. Ins. by the Constitution (Seventy-seventh Amendment) Act, 1995, s. 2 '
  '(w.e.f. 17-6-1995).\n'
  '\n'
  '3\\. Subs. by the Constitution (Eighty-fifth Amendment) Act, 2001, s. 2, '
  'for certain words\n'
  '(retrospectively) (w.e.f. 17-6-1995).\n'
  '\n'
  '4\\. Ins. by the Constitution (Eighty-first Amendment) Act, 2000, s. 2 '
  '(w.e.f. 9-6-2000).\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="9" -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '### (Part III .- Fundamental Rights)\n'
  '\n'
  '(5) Nothing in this article shall affect the operation of any law which\n'
  'provides that the incumbent of an office in connection with the affairs of '
  'any\n'
  'religious or denominational institution or any member of the governing '
  'body\n'
  'thereof shall be a person professing a particular religion or belonging to '
  'a\n'
  'particular denomination.\n'
  '\n'
  '1[(6) Nothing in this article shall prevent the State from making any\n'
  'provision for the reservation of appointments or posts in favour of any\n'
  'economically weaker sections of citizens other than the classes mentioned '
  'in\n'
  'clause (4), in addition to the existing reservation and subject to a '
  'maximum of\n'
  'ten per cent. of the posts in each category.]\n'
  '\n'
  '17\\. Abolition of Untouchability .- "Untouchability" is abolished and its\n'
  'practice in any form is forbidden. The enforcement of any disability '
  'arising out\n'
  'of "Untouchability" shall be an offence punishable in accordance with law.\n'
  '\n'
  '18\\. Abolition of titles .- (1) No title, not being a military or '
  'academic\n'
  'distinction, shall be conferred by the State.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) No citizen of India shall accept any title from any foreign State.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) No person who is not a citizen of India shall, while he holds any\n'
  'office of profit or trust under the State, accept without the consent of '
  'the\n'
  'President any title from any foreign State.\n'
  '\n'
  '(4) No person holding any office of profit or trust under the State shall,\n'
  'without the consent of the President, accept any present, emolument, or '
  'office\n'
  'of any kind from or under any foreign State.\n'
  '\n'
  'Right to Freedom\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '#### 19. Protection of certain rights regarding freedom of speech, etc .-\n'
  '\n'
  '(1) All citizens shall have the right-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) to freedom of speech and expression;\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) to assemble peaceably and without arms;\n'
  '\n'
  '(c) to form associations or unions 2[or co-operative societies ];\n'
  '\n'
  '(d) to move freely throughout the territory of India;\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Ins. by the Constitution (One Hundred and Third Amendment) Act, 2019, '
  's. 3\n'
  '(w.e.f. 14-1-2019).\n'
  '\n'
  '2\\. Ins. by the Constitution (Ninety-seventh Amendment) Act, 2011, s. 2 '
  '(w.e.f. 8-2-2012).\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'

  '\n'

  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA (Part III .- Fundamental Rights)\n'
  '\n'
  '(e) to reside and settle in any part of the territory of India; 1[and]\n'
  '2[(f)*\n'
  '*\n'
  '*\n'
  '*]\n'
  '*\n'
  '\n'
  '(g) to practise any profession, or to carry on any occupation, trade or\n'
  'business.\n'
  '\n'
  '3[(2) Nothing in sub-clause (a) of clause (1) shall affect the operation '
  'of\n'
  'any existing law, or prevent the State from making any law, in so far as '
  'such\n'
  'law imposes reasonable restrictions on the exercise of the right conferred '

  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '### (Part III .- Fundamental Rights)\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '#### Right to Constitutional Remedies\n'
  '\n'
  '32\\. Remedies for enforcement of rights conferred by this Part .- (1)\n'
  'The right to move the Supreme Court by appropriate proceedings for the\n'
  'enforcement of the rights conferred by this Part is guaranteed.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) The Supreme Court shall have power to issue directions or orders or\n'
  'writs, including writs in the nature of habeas corpus, mandamus, '
  'prohibition,\n'
  'quo warranto and certiorari, whichever may be appropriate, for the\n'
  'enforcement of any of the rights conferred by this Part.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) Without prejudice to the powers conferred on the Supreme Court by\n'
  'clauses (1) and (2), Parliament may by law empower any other court to '
  'exercise\n'
  'within the local limits of its jurisdiction all or any of the powers '
  'exercisable by\n'
  'the Supreme Court under clause (2).\n'
  '\n'
  '(4) The right guaranteed by this article shall not be suspended except as\n'
  'otherwise provided for by this Constitution.\n'
  '\n'
  '132A. [Constitutional validity of State laws not to be considered in\n'
  'proceedings under article 32.] .- Omitted by the Constitution (Forty-third\n'
  'Amendment) Act, 1977, s. 3 (w.e.f. 13-4-1978).\n'
  '\n'
  '2[33. Power of Parliament to modify the rights conferred by this Part\n'
  'in their application to Forces, etc .- Parliament may, by law, determine to '
  'what\n'
  'extent any of the rights conferred by this Part shall, in their application '
  'to,-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) the members of the Armed Forces; or\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) the members of the Forces charged with the maintenance of\n'
  'public order; or\n'
  '\n'
  '(c) persons employed in any bureau or other organisation established\n'
  'by the State for purposes of intelligence or counter intelligence; or\n'
  '\n'
  '(d) person employed in, or in connection with, the telecommunication\n'
  'systems set up for the purposes of any Force, bureau or organisation\n'
  'referred to in clauses (a) to (c),\n'
  '\n'
  'be restricted or abrogated so as to ensure the proper discharge of their '
  'duties\n'
  'and the maintenance of discipline among them.]\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Ins. by the Constitution (Forty-second Amendment) Act, 1976, s. 6 '
  '(w.e.f. 1-2-1977).\n'
  '\n'
  '2\\. Subs. by the Constitution (Fiftieth Amendment) Act, 1984, s. 2, for '
  'art. 33\n'
  '(w.e.f. 11-9-1984).\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="20" -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA (Part III .- Fundamental Rights)\n'
  '\n'
  '34\\. Restriction on rights conferred by this Part while martial law is\n'
  'in force in any area .- Notwithstanding anything in the foregoing '
  'provisions\n'
  'of this Part, Parliament may by law indemnify any person in the service of '
  'the\n'
  'Union or of a State or any other person in respect of any act done by him '
  'in\n'
  'connection with the maintenance or restoration of order in any area within '
  'the\n'
  'territory of India where martial law was in force or validate any sentence\n'
  'passed, punishment inflicted, forfeiture ordered or other act done under '
  'martial\n'
  'law in such area.\n'
  '\n'
  '35\\. Legislation to give effect to the provisions of this Part .-\n'
  'Notwithstanding anything in this Constitution,-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) Parliament shall have, and the Legislature of a State shall not\n'
  'have, power to make laws-\n'
  '\n'
  '(i) with respect to any of the matters which under clause (3) of\n'
  'article 16, clause (3) of article 32, article 33 and article 34 may be\n'
  'provided for by law made by Parliament; and\n'
  '\n'
  '(ii) for prescribing punishment for those acts which are declared\n'
  'to be offences under this Part,\n'
  '\n'
  'and Parliament shall, as soon as may be after the commencement of this\n'
  'Constitution, make laws for prescribing punishment for the acts referred\n'
  'to in sub-clause (ii);\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) any law in force immediately before the commencement of this\n'
  'Constitution in the territory of India with respect to any of the matters\n'
  'referred to in sub-clause (i) of clause (a) or providing for punishment '
  'for\n'
  'any act referred to in sub-clause (ii) of that clause shall, subject to '
  'the\n'
  'terms thereof and to any adaptations and modifications that may be made\n'
  'therein under article 372, continue in force until altered or repealed or\n'
  'amended by Parliament.\n'
  '\n'
  'Explanation .- In this article, the expression "law in force" has the same\n'
  'meaning as in article 372.\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## PART IV DIRECTIVE PRINCIPLES OF STATE POLICY\n'
  '\n'
  '36\\. Definition .- In this Part, unless the context otherwise requires, '
  '"the\n'
  'State" has the same meaning as in Part III.\n'
  '\n'
  '37\\. Application of the principles contained in this Part .- The\n'
  'provisions contained in this Part shall not be enforceable by any court, '
  'but the\n'
  'principles therein laid down are nevertheless fundamental in the governance '
  'of\n'
  'the country and it shall be the duty of the State to apply these principles '
  'in\n'
  'making laws.\n'
  '\n'
  '38\\. State to secure a social order for the promotion of welfare of the\n'
  'people .- 1[(1)] The State shall strive to promote the welfare of the '
  'people by\n'
  'securing and protecting as effectively as it may a social order in which '
  'justice,\n'
  'social, economic and political, shall inform all the institutions of the '
  'national life.\n'
  '\n'
  '2[(2) The State shall, in particular, strive to minimise the inequalities '
  'in\n'
  'income, and endeavour to eliminate inequalities in status, facilities and\n'
  'opportunities, not only amongst individuals but also amongst groups of '
  'people\n'
  'residing in different areas or engaged in different vocations.]\n'
  '\n'
  '39\\. Certain principles of policy to be followed by the State .- The\n'
  'State shall, in particular, direct its policy towards securing-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) that the citizens, men and women equally, have the right to an\n'
  'adequate means of livelihood;\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) that the ownership and control of the material resources of the\n'
  'community are so distributed as best to subserve the common good;\n'
  '\n'
  '(c) that the operation of the economic system does not result in the\n'
  'concentration of wealth and means of production to the common\n'
  'detriment;\n'
  '\n'
  '(d) that there is equal pay for equal work for both men and women;\n'
  '\n'
  '(e) that the health and strength of workers, men and women, and\n'
  'the tender age of children are not abused and that citizens are not forced\n'
  'by economic necessity to enter avocations unsuited to their age or\n'
  'strength;\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Art. 38 renumbered as cl. (1) by the Constitution (Forty-fourth '
  'Amendment) Act,\n'
  '1978, s. 9 (w.e.f. 20-6-1979).\n'
  '\n'
  '2\\. Ins. by s. 9, ibid. (w.e.f. 20-6-1979).\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="21" -->\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="22" -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## (Part IV .- Directive Principles of State Policy)\n'
  '\n'
  '1[(f) that children are given opportunities and facilities to develop\n'
  '☒\n'
  'in a healthy manner and in conditions of freedom and dignity and that\n'
  'childhood and youth are protected against exploitation and against moral\n'
  'and material abandonment.]\n'
  '\n'
  '2[39A. Equal justice and free legal aid .- The State shall secure that the\n'
  'operation of the legal system promotes justice, on a basis of equal '
  'opportunity,\n'
  'and shall, in particular, provide free legal aid, by suitable legislation '
  'or schemes\n'
  'or in any other way, to ensure that opportunities for securing justice are '
  'not\n'
  'denied to any citizen by reason of economic or other disabilities.]\n',

  'Legislation to give effect to the provisions of this Part.\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## PART IV\n'
  '\n'
  'DIRECTIVE PRINCIPLES OF STATE POLICY\n',
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA (Part III .- Fundamental Rights)\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that nothing in this sub-clause shall authorise the detention\n'
  'of any person beyond the maximum period prescribed by any law made\n'
  'by Parliament under sub-clause (b) of clause (7); or\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) such person is detained in accordance with the provisions of any\n'
  'law made by Parliament under sub-clauses (a) and (b) of clause (7).\n'
  '\n'
  '(5) When any person is detained in pursuance of an order made under\n'
  'any law providing for preventive detention, the authority making the order\n'
  'shall, as soon as may be, communicate to such person the grounds on which '
  'the\n'
  'order has been made and shall afford him the earliest opportunity of making '
  'a\n'
  'representation against the order.\n'
  '\n'
  '(6) Nothing in clause (5) shall require the authority making any such\n'
  'order as is referred to in that clause to disclose facts which such '
  'authority\n'
  'considers to be against the public interest to disclose.\n'
  '\n'
  '(7) Parliament may by law prescribe-\n'
  '\n'
  '"(a) the circumstances under which, and the class or classes of cases\n'
  'in which, a person may be detained for a period longer than three months\n'
  'under any law providing for preventive detention without obtaining the\n'
  'opinion of an Advisory Board in accordance with the provisions of\n'
  'sub-clause (a) of clause (4);\n'
  '\n'
  '** (b) the maximum period for which any person may in any class or\n'
  'classes of cases be detained under any law providing for preventive\n'
  'detention; and\n'
  '\n'
  '*** (c) the procedure to be followed by an Advisory Board in an\n'
  'inquiry under **** sub-clause (a) of clause (4).\n'
  '\n'
  '\\* Sub-clause (a) shall stand omitted by the Constitution (Forty-fourth '
  'Amendment) Act,\n'
  '1978, s. 3(b)(i) (date to be notified).\n'
  '\n'
  '** Sub-clause (b) shall stand re-lettered as sub-clause (a) by s. 3(b)(ii), '
  'ibid. (date to be\n'
  'notified).\n'
  '\n'
  '*** Sub-clause (c) shall stand re-lettered as sub-clause (b) by s. '
  '3(b)(iii), ibid. (date to be\n'
  'notified).\n'
  '\n'
  '**** Sub-clause (a) of clause (4) shall stand substituted as "clause (4)" '
  'by s. 3(b)(iii),\n'
  'ibid. (date to be notified).\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="14" -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '### (Part III .- Fundamental Rights)\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '#### Right against Exploitation\n'
  '\n'
  '23\\. Prohibition of traffic in human beings and forced labour .- (1)\n'
  'Traffic in human beings and begar and other similar forms of forced labour '
  'are\n'
  'prohibited and any contravention of this provision shall be an offence\n'
  'punishable in accordance with law.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) Nothing in this article shall prevent the State from imposing\n'
  'compulsory service for public purposes, and in imposing such service the '
  'State\n'
  'shall not make any discrimination on grounds only of religion, race, caste '
  'or\n'
  'class or any of them.\n'
  '\n'
  '24\\. Prohibition of employment of children in factories, etc .- No child\n'
  'below the age of fourteen years shall be employed to work in any factory '
  'or\n'
  'mine or engaged in any other hazardous employment.\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '##### Right to Freedom of Religion\n'
  '\n'
  '25\\. Freedom of conscience and free profession, practice and\n'
  'propagation of religion .- (1) Subject to public order, morality and health '
  'and\n'
  'to the other provisions of this Part, all persons are equally entitled to '
  'freedom\n'
  'of conscience and the right freely to profess, practice and propagate '
  'religion.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) Nothing in this article shall affect the operation of any existing law '
  'or\n'
  'prevent the State from making any law-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) regulating or restricting any economic, financial, political or\n'
  'other secular activity which may be associated with religious practice;\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) providing for social welfare and reform or the throwing open\n'
  'of Hindu religious institutions of a public character to all classes and\n'
  'sections of Hindus.\n'
  '\n'
  'Explanation I .- The wearing and carrying of kirpans shall be deemed to\n'
  'be included in the profession of the Sikh religion.\n'
  '\n'
  'Explanation II .- In sub-clause (b) of clause (2), the reference to Hindus\n'
  'shall be construed as including a reference to persons professing the Sikh, '
  'Jaina\n'
  'or Buddhist religion, and the reference to Hindu religious institutions '
  'shall be\n'
  'construed accordingly.\n'
  '\n'
  '26\\. Freedom to manage religious affairs .- Subject to public order,\n'
  'morality and health, every religious denomination or any section thereof '
  'shall\n'
  'have the right-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) to establish and maintain institutions for religious and charitable\n'
  'purposes;\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="15" -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '### (Part III .- Fundamental Rights)\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) to manage its own affairs in matters of religion;\n'
  '\n'
  '(c) to own and acquire movable and immovable property; and\n'
  '\n'
  '(d) to administer such property in accordance with law.\n'
  '\n'
  '27\\. Freedom as to payment of taxes for promotion of any particular\n'
  'religion .- No person shall be compelled to pay any taxes, the proceeds of\n'
  'which are specifically appropriated in payment of expenses for the '
  'promotion\n'
  'or maintenance of any particular religion or religious denomination.\n'
  '\n'
  '28\\. Freedom as to attendance at religious instruction or religious\n'
  'worship in certain educational institutions .- (1) No religious '
  'instruction\n'
  'shall be provided in any educational institution wholly maintained out of '
  'State\n'
  'funds.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) Nothing in clause (1) shall apply to an educational institution which\n'
  'is administered by the State but has been established under any endowment '
  'or\n'
  'trust which requires that religious instruction shall be imparted in such\n'
  'institution.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) No person attending any educational institution recognised by the\n'
  'State or receiving aid out of State funds shall be required to take part in '
  'any\n'
  'religious instruction that may be imparted in such institution or to attend '
  'any\n'
  'religious worship that may be conducted in such institution or in any '
  'premises\n'
  'attached thereto unless such person or, if such person is a minor, his '
  'guardian\n'
  'has given his consent thereto.\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '#### Cultural and Educational Rights\n'
  '\n'
  '29\\. Protection of interests of minorities .- (1) Any section of the\n'
  'citizens residing in the territory of India or any part thereof having a '
  'distinct\n'
  'language, script or culture of its own shall have the right to conserve the '
  'same.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) No citizen shall be denied admission into any educational institution\n'
  'maintained by the State or receiving aid out of State funds on grounds only '
  'of\n'
  'religion, race, caste, language or any of them.\n'
  '\n'
  '30\\. Right of minorities to establish and administer educational\n'
  'institutions .- (1) All minorities, whether based on religion or language, '
  'shall\n'
  'have the right to establish and administer educational institutions of '
  'their\n'
  'choice.\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="16" -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '### (Part III .- Fundamental Rights)\n'
  '\n'
  '1[(1A) In making any law providing for the compulsory acquisition of\n'
  'any property of an educational institution established and administered by '
  'a\n'
  'minority, referred to in clause (1), the State shall ensure that the amount '
  'fixed\n'
  'by or determined under such law for the acquisition of such property is '
  'such as\n'
  'would not restrict or abrogate the right guaranteed under that clause.]\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) The State shall not, in granting aid to educational institutions,\n'
  'discriminate against any educational institution on the ground that it is '
  'under\n'
  'the management of a minority, whether based on religion or language.\n'
  '\n'

  '\n'
  '## PART II CITIZENSHIP\n'
  '\n'
  '5\\. Citizenship at the commencement of the Constitution .- At the\n'
  'commencement of this Constitution, every person who has his domicile in '
  'the\n'
  'territory of India and-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) who was born in the territory of India; or\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) either of whose parents was born in the territory of India; or\n'
  '\n'
  '(c) who has been ordinarily resident in the territory of India for\n'
  'not less than five years immediately preceding such commencement,\n'
  'shall be a citizen of India.\n'
  '\n'
  '6\\. Rights of citizenship of certain persons who have migrated to\n'
  'India from Pakistan .- Notwithstanding anything in article 5, a person who\n'
  'has migrated to the territory of India from the territory now included in\n'
  'Pakistan shall be deemed to be a citizen of India at the commencement of '
  'this\n'
  'Constitution if-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) he or either of his parents or any of his grand-parents was born\n'
  'in India as defined in the Government of India Act, 1935 (as originally\n'
  'enacted); and\n'
  '\n'
  '(b)(i) in the case where such person has so migrated before the\n'
  'nineteenth day of July, 1948, he has been ordinarily resident in the\n'
  'territory of India since the date of his migration, or\n'
  '\n'
  '(ii) in the case where such person has so migrated on or after the\n'
  'nineteenth day of July, 1948, he has been registered as a citizen of India\n'
  'by an officer appointed in that behalf by the Government of the\n'
  'Dominion of India on an application made by him therefor to such\n'
  'officer before the commencement of this Constitution in the form and\n'
  'manner prescribed by that Government:\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that no person shall be so registered unless he has been resident\n'
  'in the territory of India for at least six months immediately preceding the '
  'date\n'
  'of his application.\n'
  '\n'
  '7\\. Rights of citizenship of certain migrants to Pakistan .-\n'
  'Notwithstanding anything in articles 5 and 6, a person who has after the '
  'first\n'
  'day of March, 1947, migrated from the territory of India to the territory '
  'now\n'
  'included in Pakistan shall not be deemed to be a citizen of India:\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="4" -->\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="5" -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '### (Part II .- Citizenship)\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that nothing in this article shall apply to a person who, after\n'
  'having so migrated to the territory now included in Pakistan, has returned '
  'to the\n'
  'territory of India under a permit for resettlement or permanent return '
  'issued by\n'
  'or under the authority of any law and every such person shall for the '
  'purposes\n'
  'of clause (b) of article 6 be deemed to have migrated to the territory of '
  'India\n'
  'after the nineteenth day of July, 1948.\n'
  '\n'
  '8\\. Rights of citizenship of certain persons of Indian origin residing\n'
  'outside India .- Notwithstanding anything in article 5, any person who or\n'
  'either of whose parents or any of whose grand-parents was born in India as\n'
  'defined in the Government of India Act, 1935 (as originally enacted), and '
  'who\n'
  'is ordinarily residing in any country outside India as so defined shall be '
  'deemed\n'
  'to be a citizen of India if he has been registered as a citizen of India by '
  'the\n'
  'diplomatic or consular representative of India in the country where he is '
  'for the\n'
  'time being residing on an application made by him therefor to such '
  'diplomatic\n'
  'or consular representative, whether before or after the commencement of '
  'this\n'
  'Constitution, in the form and manner prescribed by the Government of the\n'
  'Dominion of India or the Government of India.\n'
  '\n'
  '9\\. Persons voluntarily acquiring citizenship of a foreign State not to\n'
  'be citizens .- No person shall be a citizen of India by virtue of article '
  '5, or be\n'
  'deemed to be a citizen of India by virtue of article 6 or article 8, if he '
  'has\n'
  'voluntarily acquired the citizenship of any foreign State.\n'
  '\n'
  '10\\. Continuance of the rights of citizenship .- Every person who is or\n'
  'is deemed to be a citizen of India under any of the foregoing provisions of '
  'this\n'
  'Part shall, subject to the provisions of any law that may be made by '
  'Parliament,\n'
  'continue to be such citizen.\n'
  '\n'
  '11\\. Parliament to regulate the right of citizenship by law .- Nothing\n'
  'in the foregoing provisions of this Part shall derogate from the power of\n'
  'Parliament to make any provision with respect to the acquisition and\n'
  'termination of citizenship and all other matters relating to citizenship.\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## PART III FUNDAMENTAL RIGHTS\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '### General\n'
  '\n'
  '12\\. Definition .- In this Part, unless the context otherwise requires, '
  '"the\n'
  'State" includes the Government and Parliament of India and the Government\n'
  'and the Legislature of each of the States and all local or other '
  'authorities within\n'
  'the territory of India or under the control of the Government of India.\n'
  '\n'
  '13\\. Laws inconsistent with or in derogation of the fundamental\n'
  'rights .- (1) All laws in force in the territory of India immediately '
  'before the\n'
  'commencement of this Constitution, in so far as they are inconsistent with '
  'the\n'
  'provisions of this Part, shall, to the extent of such inconsistency, be '
  'void.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) The State shall not make any law which takes away or abridges the\n'
  'rights conferred by this Part and any law made in contravention of this '
  'clause\n'
  'shall, to the extent of the contravention, be void.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) In this article, unless the context otherwise requires,-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) "law" includes any Ordinance, order, bye-law, rule, regulation,\n'
  'notification, custom or usage having in the territory of India the force '
  'of\n'
  'law;\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) "laws in force" includes laws passed or made by a Legislature\n'
  'or other competent authority in the territory of India before the\n'
  'commencement of this Constitution and not previously repealed,\n'
  'notwithstanding that any such law or any part thereof may not be then in\n'
  'operation either at all or in particular areas.\n'
  '\n'
  '1[(4) Nothing in this article shall apply to any amendment of this\n'
  'Constitution made under article 368.]\n'
  '\n'
  'Right to Equality\n'
  '\n'
  '14\\. Equality before law .- The State shall not deny to any person\n'
  'equality before the law or the equal protection of the laws within the '
  'territory of\n'
  'India.\n'
  '\n'
  '15\\. Prohibition of discrimination on grounds of religion, race, caste,\n'
  'sex or place of birth .- (1) The State shall not discriminate against any '
  'citizen\n'
  'on grounds only of religion, race, caste, sex, place of birth or any of '
  'them.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) No citizen shall, on grounds only of religion, race, caste, sex, place '
  'of\n'
  'birth or any of them, be subject to any disability, liability, restriction '
  'or\n'
  'condition with regard to-\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Ins. by the Constitution (Twenty-fourth Amendment) Act, 1971, s. 2 '
  '(w.e.f. 5-11-1971).\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="6" -->\n'

  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '### (Part III .- Fundamental Rights)\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) access to shops, public restaurants, hotels and places of public\n'
  'entertainment; or\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) the use of wells, tanks, bathing ghats, roads and places of\n'
  'public resort maintained wholly or partly out of State funds or dedicated\n'
  'to the use of the general public.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) Nothing in this article shall prevent the State from making any\n'
  'special provision for women and children.\n'
  '\n'
  '1[(4) Nothing in this article or in clause (2) of article 29 shall prevent '
  'the\n'
  'State from making any special provision for the advancement of any '
  'socially\n'
  'and educationally backward classes of citizens or for the Scheduled Castes '

 ['addition, variation or repeal the provisions of this Constitution under '

  '# PART XXI\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '# 1[TEMPORARY, TRANSITIONAL AND SPECIAL PROVISIONS]\n'
  '\n'
  '369\\. Temporary power to Parliament to make laws with respect to\n'
  'certain matters in the State List as if they were matters in the '
  'Concurrent\n'
  'List .- Notwithstanding anything in this Constitution, Parliament shall, '
  'during\n'
  'a period of five years from the commencement of this Constitution, have '
  'power\n'
  'to make laws with respect to the following matters as if they were '
  'enumerated\n'
  'in the Concurrent List, namely :-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) trade and commerce within a State in, and the production, supply\n'
  'and distribution of, cotton and woollen textiles, raw cotton (including\n'
  'ginned cotton and unginned cotton or kapas), cotton seed, paper\n'
  '(including newsprint), food-stuffs (including edible oilseeds and oil),\n'
  'cattle fodder (including oil-cakes and other concentrates), coal\n'
  '(including coke and derivatives of coal), iron, steel and mica;\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) offences against laws with respect to any of the matters mentioned\n'
  'in clause (a), jurisdiction and powers of all courts except the Supreme\n'
  'Court with respect to any of those matters, and fees in respect of any of\n'
  'those matters but not including fees taken in any court,\n'
  '\n'
  'but any law made by Parliament, which Parliament would not but for the\n'
  'provisions of this article have been competent to make, shall, to the '
  'extent of the\n'
  'incompetency, cease to have effect on the expiration of the said period, '
  'except as\n'
  'respects things done or omitted to be done before the expiration thereof.\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Subs. by the Constitution (Thirteenth Amendment) Act, 1962, s. 2, for '
  '"TEMPORARY\n'
  'AND TRANSITIONAL PROVISIONS" (w.e.f. 1-12-1963).\n'

  'Explanation .- For the purposes of this article, the\n'
  'Government of the State means the person for the time being recognised\n'
  'by the President as the Maharaja of Jammu and Kashmir acting on the\n'
  'advice of the Council of Ministers for the time being in office under the\n'
  "Maharaja's Proclamation dated the fifth day of March, 1948;\n"
  '\n'
  '(c) the provisions of article 1 and of this article shall apply in '
  'relation\n'
  'to that State;\n'
  '\n'
  '(d) such of the other provisions of this Constitution shall apply in\n'
  'relation to that State subject to such exceptions and modifications as the\n'
  'President may by order* specify:\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that no such order which relates to the matters specified in the\n'
  'Instrument of Accession of the State referred to in paragraph (i) of\n'
  'sub-clause (b) shall be issued except in consultation with the Government '
  'of\n'
  'the State:\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided further that no such order which relates to matters other than\n'
  'those referred to in the last preceding proviso shall be issued except with '
  'the\n'
  'concurrence of that Government.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) If the concurrence of the Government of the State referred to in\n'
  'paragraph (ii) of sub-clause (b) of clause (1) or in the second proviso to\n'
  'sub-clause (d) of that clause be given before the Constituent Assembly for '
  'the\n'
  'purpose of framing the Constitution of the State is convened, it shall be '
  'placed\n'
  'before such Assembly for such decision as it may take thereon.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) Notwithstanding anything in the foregoing provisions of this article,\n'
  'the President may, by public notification, declare that this article shall '
  'cease to\n'
  'be operative or shall be operative only with such exceptions and '
  'modifications\n'
  'and from such date as he may specify:\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that the recommendation of the 1[clause (2) of Legislative\n'
  'Assembly of the State] shall be necessary before the President issues such '
  'a\n'
  'notification.\n'
  '\n'

  '\n'
  '\n'
  '# SHORT TITLE, COMMENCEMENT, "[AUTHORITATIVE TEXT IN HINDI] AND REPEALS\n'
  '\n'
  '393\\. Short title .- This Constitution may be called the Constitution of\n'
  'India.\n'
  '\n'
  '394\\. Commencement .- This article and articles 5, 6, 7, 8, 9, 60, 324,\n'
  '366, 367, 379, 380, 388, 391, 392 and 393 shall come into force at once, '
  'and\n'
  'the remaining provisions of this Constitution shall come into force on the\n'
  'twenty-sixth day of January, 1950, which day is referred to in this '
  'Constitution\n'
  'as the commencement of this Constitution.\n'
  '\n'
  '2[394A. Authoritative text in the Hindi language .- (1) The President\n'
  'shall cause to be published under his authority,-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) the translation of this Constitution in the Hindi language,\n'
  'signed by the members of the Constituent Assembly, with such\n'
  'modifications as may be necessary to bring it in conformity with the\n'
  'language, style and terminology adopted in the authoritative texts of\n'
  'Central Acts in the Hindi language, and incorporating therein all the\n'
  'amendments of this Constitution made before such publication; and\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) the translation in the Hindi language of every amendment of\n'
  'this Constitution made in the English language.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) The translation of this Constitution and of every amendment thereof\n'
  'published under clause (1) shall be construed to have the same meaning as '
  'the\n'
  'original thereof and if any difficulty arises in so construing any part of '
  'such\n'
  'translation, the President shall cause the same to be revised suitably.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) The translation of this Constitution and of every amendment thereof\n'
  'published under this article shall be deemed to be, for all purposes, the\n'
  'authoritative text thereof in the Hindi language.]\n'
  '\n'
  '395\\. Repeals .- The Indian Independence Act, 1947, and the\n'
  'Government of India Act, 1935, together with all enactments amending or\n'
  'supplementing the latter Act, but not including the Abolition of Privy '
  'Council\n'
  'Jurisdiction Act, 1949, are hereby repealed.\n'
  '\n'

  '(w.e.f. 9-12-1987).\n'
  '\n'

  '(a) assume to himself all or any of the functions of the\n'
  'Government of the State and all or any of the powers vested in or\n'

  'other than the Legislature of the State;\n'
  '\n'

  'exercisable by or under the authority of Parliament;\n'
  '\n'
  '(c) make such incidental and consequential provisions as appear\n'
  'to the President to be necessary or desirable for giving effect to the\n'
  'objects of the Proclamation, including provisions for suspending in\n'
  'whole or in part the operation of any provisions of this Constitution\n'
  'relating to any body or authority in the State:\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that nothing in this clause shall authorise the President to\n'
  'assume to himself any of the powers vested in or exercisable by a High '
  'Court,\n'
  'or to suspend in whole or in part the operation of any provision of this\n'
  'Constitution relating to High Courts.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) Any such Proclamation may be revoked or varied by a subsequent\n'
  'Proclamation.\n'
  '\n'

  'of Parliament and shall, except where it is a Proclamation revoking a '
  'previous\n'
  'Proclamation, cease to operate at the expiration of two months unless '
  'before\n'
  'the expiration of that period it has been approved by resolutions of both '
  'Houses\n'
  'of Parliament:\n'
  '\n'

  'the\n'
  'People is dissolved or the dissolution of the House of the People takes '
  'place\n'
  'during the period of two months referred to in this clause, and if a '
  'resolution\n'
  'approving the Proclamation has been passed by the Council of States, but '
  'no\n'

  'of\n'
  'the People before the expiration of that period, the Proclamation shall '
  'cease to\n'

  'of the\n'
  'People first sits after its reconstitution unless before the expiration of '
  'the said\n'
  'period of thirty days a resolution approving the Proclamation has been '
  'also\n'
  'passed by the House of the People.\n'

  '\n'
  '## PART II CITIZENSHIP\n'
  '\n'
  '5\\. Citizenship at the commencement of the Constitution .- At the\n'
  'commencement of this Constitution, every person who has his domicile in '
  'the\n'
  'territory of India and-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) who was born in the territory of India; or\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) either of whose parents was born in the territory of India; or\n'
  '\n'
  '(c) who has been ordinarily resident in the territory of India for\n'
  'not less than five years immediately preceding such commencement,\n'
  'shall be a citizen of India.\n'
  '\n'
  '6\\. Rights of citizenship of certain persons who have migrated to\n'
  'India from Pakistan .- Notwithstanding anything in article 5, a person who\n'
  'has migrated to the territory of India from the territory now included in\n'
  'Pakistan shall be deemed to be a citizen of India at the commencement of '
  'this\n'
  'Constitution if-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) he or either of his parents or any of his grand-parents was born\n'
  'in India as defined in the Government of India Act, 1935 (as originally\n'
  'enacted); and\n'
  '\n'
  '(b)(i) in the case where such person has so migrated before the\n'
  'nineteenth day of July, 1948, he has been ordinarily resident in the\n'
  'territory of India since the date of his migration, or\n'
  '\n'
  '(ii) in the case where such person has so migrated on or after the\n'
  'nineteenth day of July, 1948, he has been registered as a citizen of India\n'
  'by an officer appointed in that behalf by the Government of the\n'
  'Dominion of India on an application made by him therefor to such\n'
  'officer before the commencement of this Constitution in the form and\n'
  'manner prescribed by that Government:\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that no person shall be so registered unless he has been resident\n'
  'in the territory of India for at least six months immediately preceding the '
  'date\n'
  'of his application.\n'
  '\n'
  '7\\. Rights of citizenship of certain migrants to Pakistan .-\n'
  'Notwithstanding anything in articles 5 and 6, a person who has after the '
  'first\n'
  'day of March, 1947, migrated from the territory of India to the territory '
  'now\n'
  'included in Pakistan shall not be deemed to be a citizen of India:\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="4" -->\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="5" -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '### (Part II .- Citizenship)\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that nothing in this article shall apply to a person who, after\n'
  'having so migrated to the territory now included in Pakistan, has returned '
  'to the\n'
  'territory of India under a permit for resettlement or permanent return '
  'issued by\n'
  'or under the authority of any law and every such person shall for the '
  'purposes\n'
  'of clause (b) of article 6 be deemed to have migrated to the territory of '
  'India\n'
  'after the nineteenth day of July, 1948.\n'
  '\n'
  '8\\. Rights of citizenship of certain persons of Indian origin residing\n'
  'outside India .- Notwithstanding anything in article 5, any person who or\n'
  'either of whose parents or any of whose grand-parents was born in India as\n'
  'defined in the Government of India Act, 1935 (as originally enacted), and '
  'who\n'
  'is ordinarily residing in any country outside India as so defined shall be '
  'deemed\n'
  'to be a citizen of India if he has been registered as a citizen of India by '
  'the\n'
  'diplomatic or consular representative of India in the country where he is '
  'for the\n'
  'time being residing on an application made by him therefor to such '
  'diplomatic\n'
  'or consular representative, whether before or after the commencement of '
  'this\n'
  'Constitution, in the form and manner prescribed by the Government of the\n'
  'Dominion of India or the Government of India.\n'
  '\n'
  '9\\. Persons voluntarily acquiring citizenship of a foreign State not to\n'
  'be citizens .- No person shall be a citizen of India by virtue of article '
  '5, or be\n'
  'deemed to be a citizen of India by virtue of article 6 or article 8, if he '
  'has\n'
  'voluntarily acquired the citizenship of any foreign State.\n'
  '\n'
  '10\\. Continuance of the rights of citizenship .- Every person who is or\n'
  'is deemed to be a citizen of India under any of the foregoing provisions of '
  'this\n'
  'Part shall, subject to the provisions of any law that may be made by '
  'Parliament,\n'
  'continue to be such citizen.\n'
  '\n'
  '11\\. Parliament to regulate the right of citizenship by law .- Nothing\n'
  'in the foregoing provisions of this Part shall derogate from the power of\n'
  'Parliament to make any provision with respect to the acquisition and\n'
  'termination of citizenship and all other matters relating to citizenship.\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## PART III FUNDAMENTAL RIGHTS\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '### General\n'
  '\n'
  '12\\. Definition .- In this Part, unless the context otherwise requires, '
  '"the\n'
  'State" includes the Government and Parliament of India and the Government\n'
  'and the Legislature of each of the States and all local or other '
  'authorities within\n'
  'the territory of India or under the control of the Government of India.\n'
  '\n'
  '13\\. Laws inconsistent with or in derogation of the fundamental\n'
  'rights .- (1) All laws in force in the territory of India immediately '
  'before the\n'
  'commencement of this Constitution, in so far as they are inconsistent with '
  'the\n'
  'provisions of this Part, shall, to the extent of such inconsistency, be '
  'void.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) The State shall not make any law which takes away or abridges the\n'
  'rights conferred by this Part and any law made in contravention of this '
  'clause\n'
  'shall, to the extent of the contravention, be void.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) In this article, unless the context otherwise requires,-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) "law" includes any Ordinance, order, bye-law, rule, regulation,\n'
  'notification, custom or usage having in the territory of India the force '
  'of\n'
  'law;\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) "laws in force" includes laws passed or made by a Legislature\n'
  'or other competent authority in the territory of India before the\n'
  'commencement of this Constitution and not previously repealed,\n'
  'notwithstanding that any such law or any part thereof may not be then in\n'
  'operation either at all or in particular areas.\n'
  '\n'
  '1[(4) Nothing in this article shall apply to any amendment of this\n'
  'Constitution made under article 368.]\n'
  '\n'
  'Right to Equality\n'
  '\n'
  '14\\. Equality before law .- The State shall not deny to any person\n'
  'equality before the law or the equal protection of the laws within the '
  'territory of\n'
  'India.\n'
  '\n'
  '15\\. Prohibition of discrimination on grounds of religion, race, caste,\n'
  'sex or place of birth .- (1) The State shall not discriminate against any '
  'citizen\n'
  'on grounds only of religion, race, caste, sex, place of birth or any of '
  'them.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) No citizen shall, on grounds only of religion, race, caste, sex, place '
  'of\n'
  'birth or any of them, be subject to any disability, liability, restriction '
  'or\n'
  'condition with regard to-\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Ins. by the Constitution (Twenty-fourth Amendment) Act, 1971, s. 2 '
  '(w.e.f. 5-11-1971).\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="6" -->\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="7" -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '### (Part III .- Fundamental Rights)\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) access to shops, public restaurants, hotels and places of public\n'
  'entertainment; or\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) the use of wells, tanks, bathing ghats, roads and places of\n'
  'public resort maintained wholly or partly out of State funds or dedicated\n'
  'to the use of the general public.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) Nothing in this article shall prevent the State from making any\n'
  'special provision for women and children.\n'
  '\n'
  '1[(4) Nothing in this article or in clause (2) of article 29 shall prevent '
  'the\n'
  'State from making any special provision for the advancement of any '
  'socially\n'
  'and educationally backward classes of citizens or for the Scheduled Castes '
  'and\n'
  'the Scheduled Tribes.]\n'
  '\n'
  '2[(5) Nothing in this article or in sub-clause (g) of clause (1) of article '
  '19\n',
  '53 (w.e.f. 3-1-1977).\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="217" -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA (Part XVIII .- EMERGENCY PROVISIONS)\n'
  '\n'
  '1[(1B) Nothing in clause (1A) shall apply-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) to any law which does not contain a recital to the effect that\n'
  'such law is in relation to the Proclamation of Emergency in operation\n'
  'when it is made; or\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) to any executive action taken otherwise than under a law\n'
  'containing such a recital.]\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) An order made as aforesaid may extend to the whole or any part of\n'
  'the territory of India:\n'
  '\n'
  '2[Provided that where a Proclamation of Emergency is in operation only\n'
  'in a part of the territory of India, any such order shall not extend to any '
  'other\n'
  'part of the territory of India unless the President, being satisfied that '
  'the\n'
  'security of India or any part of the territory thereof is threatened by '
  'activities in\n'
  'or in relation to the part of the territory of India in which the '
  'Proclamation of\n'
  'Emergency is in operation, considers such extension to be necessary.]\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) Every order made under clause (1) shall, as soon as may be after it is\n'
  'made, be laid before each House of Parliament.\n'
  '\n'
  '3359A. [Application of this Part to the State of Punjab.] .- Omitted by\n'
  'the Constitution (Sixty-third Amendment) Act, 1989, s. 3 (w.e.f. '
  '6-1-1990).\n'
  '\n'
  '360\\. Provisions as to financial emergency .- (1) If the President is\n'
  'satisfied that a situation has arisen whereby the financial stability or '
  'credit of\n'
  'India or of any part of the territory thereof is threatened, he may by a\n'
  'Proclamation make a declaration to that effect.\n'
  '\n'
  '4[(2) A Proclamation issued under clause (1)-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) may be revoked or varied by a subsequent Proclamation;\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) shall be laid before each House of Parliament;\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Ins. by the Constitution (Forty-fourth Amendment) Act, 1978, s. 40 '
  '(w.e.f. 20-6-1979).\n'
  '\n'
  '2\\. Added by the Constitution (Forty-second Amendment) Act, 1976, s. 53 '
  '(w.e.f. 3-1-1977).\n'
  '\n'
  '3\\. Ins. by the Constitution (Fifty-ninth Amendment) Act, 1988, s. 3 '
  '(w.e.f. 30-3-1988)\n'
  'and ceased to operate on the expiry of a period of two years from the '
  'commencement\n'
  'of that Act, i.e. 30th day of March, 1988.\n'
  '\n'
  '4\\. Subs. by the Constitution (Forty-fourth Amendment) Act, 1978, s. 41, '
  'for cl. (2)\n'
  '(w.e.f. 20-6-1979).\n'

  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA (Part XVIII .- EMERGENCY PROVISIONS)\n'
  '\n'
  '(c) shall cease to operate at the expiration of two months, unless\n'
  'before the expiration of that period it has been approved by resolutions\n'
  'of both Houses of Parliament:\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that if any such Proclamation is issued at a time when the\n'
  'House of the People has been dissolved or the dissolution of the House of '
  'the\n'
  'People takes place during the period of two months referred to in\n'
  'sub-clause (c), and if a resolution approving the Proclamation has been '
  'passed\n'
  'by the Council of States, but no resolution with respect to such '
  'Proclamation\n'
  'has been passed by the House of the People before the expiration of that '
  'period,\n'
  'the Proclamation shall cease to operate at the expiration of thirty days '
  'from the\n'
  'date on which the House of the People first sits after its reconstitution '
  'unless\n'
  'before the expiration of the said period of thirty days a resolution '
  'approving the\n'
  'Proclamation has been also passed by the House of the People.]\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) During the period any such Proclamation as is mentioned in\n'
  'clause (1) is in operation, the executive authority of the Union shall '
  'extend to\n'
  'the giving of directions to any State to observe such canons of financial\n'
  'propriety as may be specified in the directions, and to the giving of such '
  'other\n'
  'directions as the President may deem necessary and adequate for the '
  'purpose.\n'
  '\n'
  '(4) Notwithstanding anything in this Constitution-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) any such direction may include-\n'
  '\n'
  '(i) a provision requiring the reduction of salaries and allowances\n'
  'of all or any class of persons serving in connection with the affairs of\n'
  'a State;\n'
  '\n'
  '(ii) a provision requiring all Money Bills or other Bills to which\n'
  'the provisions of article 207 apply to be reserved for the\n'
  'consideration of the President after they are passed by the Legislature\n'
  'of the State;\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) it shall be competent for the President during the period any\n'
  'Proclamation issued under this article is in operation to issue directions\n'
  'for the reduction of salaries and allowances of all or any class of '
  'persons\n'
  'serving in connection with the affairs of the Union including the Judges\n'
  'of the Supreme Court and the High Courts.\n'

  '### PART XIX MISCELLANEOUS\n'
  '\n'
  '361\\. Protection of President and Governors and Rajpramukhs .- (1)\n'
  'The President, or the Governor or Rajpramukh of a State, shall not be\n'
  'answerable to any court for the exercise and performance of the powers and\n'
  'duties of his office or for any act done or purporting to be done by him in '
  'the\n'
  'exercise and performance of those powers and duties:\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that the conduct of the President may be brought under review\n'
  'by any court, tribunal or body appointed or designated by either House of\n'
  'Parliament for the investigation of a charge under article 61:\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided further that nothing in this clause shall be construed as\n'
  'restricting the right of any person to bring appropriate proceedings '
  'against the\n'
  'Government of India or the Government of a State.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) No criminal proceedings whatsoever shall be instituted or continued\n'
  'against the President, or the Governor 1 *** of a State, in any court '
  'during his\n'
  'term of office.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) No process for the arrest or imprisonment of the President, or the\n'
  'Governor 1 *** of a State, shall issue from any court during his term of '
  'office.\n'
  '\n'
  '(4) No civil proceedings in which relief is claimed against the President,\n'
  'or the Governor 1 *** of a State, shall be instituted during his term of '
  'office in\n'
  'any court in respect of any act done or purporting to be done by him in '
  'his\n'
  'personal capacity, whether before or after he entered upon his office as\n'
  'President, or as Governor 1 *** of such State, until the expiration of two '
  'months\n'
  'next after notice in writing has been delivered to the President or the '
  'Governor\n'
  '1 *** , as the case may be, or left at his office stating the nature of '
  'the\n'
  'proceedings, the cause of action therefor, the name, description and place '
  'of\n'
  'residence of the party by whom such proceedings are to be instituted and '
  'the\n'
  'relief which he claims.\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. The words "or Rajpramukh" omitted by the Constitution (Seventh '
  'Amendment)\n'
  'Act, 1956, s. 29 and Sch. (w.e.f. 1-11-1956).\n'

  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## PREAMBLE\n'
  '\n'
  'WE, THE PEOPLE OF INDIA, having solemnly resolved to constitute\n'
  'India into a 1[SOVEREIGN SOCIALIST SECULAR DEMOCRATIC\n'
  'REPUBLIC] and to secure to all its citizens:\n'
  '\n'
  'JUSTICE, social, economic and political;\n'
  '\n'
  'LIBERTY of thought, expression, belief, faith and worship;\n'
  'EQUALITY of status and of opportunity;\n'
  '\n'
  'and to promote among them all\n'
  '\n'
  'FRATERNITY assuring the dignity of the individual and the 2[unity\n'
  'and integrity of the Nation];\n'
  '\n'
  'IN OUR CONSTITUENT ASSEMBLY this twenty-sixth day of\n'
  'November, 1949, do HEREBY ADOPT, ENACT AND GIVE TO\n'
  'OURSELVES THIS CONSTITUTION.\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Subs. by the Constitution (Forty-second Amendment) Act, 1976, s.2, for '
  '"SOVEREIGN\n'
  'DEMOCRATIC REPUBLIC" (w.e.f. 3-1-1977).\n'
  '\n'
  '2\\. Subs. by s. 2, ibid., for "Unity of the Nation" (w.e.f. 3-1-1977).\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## PART I THE UNION AND ITS TERRITORY\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Name and territory of the Union .- (1) India, that is Bharat,\n'
  'shall be a Union of States.\n'
  '\n'
  '1[(2) The States and the territories thereof shall be as specified in\n'
  'the First Schedule.]\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) The territory of India shall comprise\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) the territories of the States;\n'
  '\n'
  '2[(b) the Union territories specified in the First Schedule;\n'
  'and]\n'
  '\n'
  '(c) such other territories as may be acquired.\n'
  '\n'
  '2\\. Admission or establishment of new States .- Parliament may\n'
  'by law admit into the Union, or establish, new States on such terms and\n'
  'conditions as it thinks fit.\n'
  '\n'
  '3[2A. [Sikkim to be associated with the Union.] .- Omitted by the\n'
  'Constitution (Thirty-sixth Amendment) Act, 1975, s. 5 (w.e.f. 26-4-1975).]\n'
  '\n'
  '3\\. Formation of new States and alteration of areas,\n'
  'boundaries or names of existing States .- Parliament may by law-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) form a new State by separation of territory from any\n'
  'State or by uniting two or more States or parts of States or by\n'
  'uniting any territory to a part of any State;\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) increase the area of any State;\n'
  '\n'
  '(c) diminish the area of any State;\n'
  '\n'
  '(d) alter the boundaries of any State;\n'
  '\n'
  '(e) alter the name of any State:\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Subs. by the Constitution (Seventh Amendment) Act, 1956, s. 2, for cl. '
  '(2)\n'
  '(w.e.f. 1-11-1956).\n'
  '\n'
  '2\\. Subs. by s. 2 ibid. for sub-clause (b) (w.e.f. 1-11-1956).\n'
  '\n'
  '3\\. Ins. by the Constitution (Thirty-fifth Amendment) Act, 1974, s. 2 '
  '(w.e.f. 1-3-1975).\n'
  '\n'

  'uniting a part of any State or Union territory to any other State or\n'
  'Union territory.]\n'

  '(including provisions as to representation in Parliament and in the\n'
  'Legislature or Legislatures of the State or States affected by such law)\n'
  'as Parliament may deem necessary.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) No such law as aforesaid shall be deemed to be an\n'
  'amendment of this Constitution for the purposes of article 368.\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Subs. by the Constitution (Fifth Amendment) Act, 1955, s. 2, for the '
  'proviso\n'
  '(w.e.f. 24-12-1955).\n'

  'Schedule" omitted by the\n'

  '## PREFACE\n'
  '\n'
  'This is the sixth pocket size edition of the Constitution of\n'
  'India in the diglot form. In this edition, the text of the\n'
  'Constitution of India has been brought up-to-date by\n'
  'incorporating therein all the amendments up to the Constitution\n'
  '(One Hundred and Sixth Amendment) Act, 2023. The foot notes\n'
  'below the text indicate the Constitution Amendment Acts by\n'
  'which such amendments have been made.\n'
  '\n'
  'The Constitution (One Hundredth Amendment) Act, 2015\n'
  'containing details of acquired and transferred territories\n'
  'between the Governments of India and Bangladesh has been\n'
  'provided in Appendix I.\n'
  '\n'
  'The Constitution (Application to Jammu and Kashmir)\n'
  'Order, 2019 and the declaration under article 370(3) of the\n'
  'Constitution have been provided respectively in Appendix II and\n'
  'Appendix III for reference.\n'

  '\n'
  'PREAMBLE\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## PART I\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## THE UNION AND ITS TERRITORY\n'
  '\n'
  'ARTICLES\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\.\n'
  'Name and territory of the Union.\n'
  '\n'
  '2\\.\n'
  'Admission or establishment of new States.\n'
  '\n'
  '[2A.\n'
  'Sikkim to be associated with the Union .- Omitted.]\n'
  '\n'
  '3\\.\n'
  'Formation of new States and alteration of areas, boundaries or\n'
  'names of existing States.\n'
  '\n'
  '4\\.\n'
  'Laws made under articles 2 and 3 to provide for the amendment of\n'
  'the First and the Fourth Schedules and supplemental, incidental\n'
  'and consequential matters.\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'

  '\n'

  '\n'
  '6\\.\n'
  'Rights of citizenship of certain persons who have migrated to\n'
  'India from Pakistan.\n'
  '\n'
  '7\\.\n'
  'Rights of citizenship of certain migrants to Pakistan.\n'
  '\n'
  '8\\.\n'
  'Rights of citizenship of certain persons of Indian origin residing\n'
  'outside India.\n'
  '\n'
  '9\\.\n'
  'Persons voluntarily acquiring citizenship of a foreign State not to\n'
  'be citizens.\n'
  '\n'
  '10\\.\n'
  'Continuance of the rights of citizenship.\n'
  '\n'
  '11\\.\n'
  'Parliament to regulate the right of citizenship by law.\n'

  'Parliament may make such provision as it thinks fit for the discharge of '
  'the\n'
  'functions of the President in any contingency not provided for in this '
  'Chapter.\n'
  '\n'
  '1[71. Matters relating to, or connected with, the election of a\n'
  'President or Vice-President .- (1) All doubts and disputes arising out of '
  'or in\n'
  'connection with the election of a President or Vice-President shall be '
  'inquired\n'
  'into and decided by the Supreme Court whose decision shall be final.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) If the election of a person as President or Vice-President is declared\n'
  'void by the Supreme Court, acts done by him in the exercise and '
  'performance\n'
  'of the powers and duties of the office of President or Vice-President, as '
  'the\n'
  'case may be, on or before the date of the decision of the Supreme Court '
  'shall\n'
  'not be invalidated by reason of that declaration.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) Subject to the provisions of this Constitution, Parliament may by law\n'
  'regulate any matter relating to or connected with the election of a '
  'President or\n'
  'Vice-President.\n'
  '\n'
  '(4) The election of a person as President or Vice-President shall not be\n'
  'called in question on the ground of the existence of any vacancy for '
  'whatever\n'
  'reason among the members of the electoral college electing him.]\n'
  '\n'
  '72\\. Power of President to grant pardons, etc., and to suspend, remit\n'
  'or commute sentences in certain cases .- (1) The President shall have the\n'
  'power to grant pardons, reprieves, respites or remissions of punishment or '
  'to\n'
  'suspend, remit or commute the sentence of any person convicted of any\n'
  'offence-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) in all cases where the punishment or sentence is by a Court\n'
  'Martial;\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Subs. by the Constitution (Thirty-ninth Amendment) Act, 1975, s. 2 '
  '(w.e.f 10-8-1975) and\n'
  'further subs. by the Constitution (Forty-fourth Amendment) Act, 1978, s. '
  '10.\n'
  '(w.e.f. 20-6-1979).\n'

  '(Part V .- The Union)\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) in all cases where the punishment or sentence is for an offence\n'
  'against any law relating to a matter to which the executive power of the\n'
  'Union extends;\n'
  '\n'
  '(c) in all cases where the sentence is a sentence of death.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) Nothing in sub-clause (a) of clause (1) shall affect the power\n'
  'conferred by law on any officer of the Armed Forces of the Union to '
  'suspend,\n'
  'remit or commute a sentence passed by a Court Martial.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) Nothing in sub-clause (c) of clause (1) shall affect the power to\n'
  'suspend, remit or commute a sentence of death exercisable by the Governor 1 '
  '***\n'
  'of a State under any law for the time being in force.\n'
  '\n'
  '73\\. Extent of executive power of the Union .- (1) Subject to the\n'
  'provisions of this Constitution, the executive power of the Union shall '
  'extend\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) to the matters with respect to which Parliament has power to make\n'
  'laws; and\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) to the exercise of such rights, authority and jurisdiction as are\n'
  'exercisable by the Government of India by virtue of any treaty or\n'
  'agreement:\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that the executive power referred to in sub-clause (a) shall not,\n'
  'save as expressly provided in this Constitution or in any law made by '
  'Parliament,\n'
  'extend in any State 2 *** to matters with respect to which the Legislature '
  'of the\n'
  'State has also power to make laws.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) Until otherwise provided by Parliament, a State and any officer or\n'
  'authority of a State may, notwithstanding anything in this article, '
  'continue to\n'
  'exercise in matters with respect to which Parliament has power to make laws '
  'for\n'
  'that State such executive power or functions as the State or officer or '
  'authority\n'
  'thereof could exercise immediately before the commencement of this\n'
  'Constitution.\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. The words "or Rajpramukh" omitted by the Constitution (Seventh '
  'Amendment) Act,\n'
  '1956, s. 29 and Sch. (w.e.f. 1-11-1956).\n'
  '\n'
  '2\\. The words and letters "specified in Part A or Part B of the First '
  'Schedule" omitted by\n'
  'the Constitution (Seventh Amendment) Act, 1956, s. 29 and Sch. (w.e.f. '
  '1-11-1956).\n'

  '#### Council of Ministers\n'
  '\n'
  '74\\. Council of Ministers to aid and advise President .- 1[(1) There '
  'shall\n'
  'be a Council of Ministers with the Prime Minister at the head to aid and '
  'advise\n'
  'the President who shall, in the exercise of his functions, act in '
  'accordance with\n'
  'such advice:]\n'
  '\n'
  '2[Provided that the President may require the Council of Ministers to\n'
  'reconsider such advice, either generally or otherwise, and the President '
  'shall act\n'
  'in accordance with the advice tendered after such reconsideration.]\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) The question whether any, and if so what, advice was tendered by\n'
  'Ministers to the President shall not be inquired into in any court.\n'
  '\n'
  '75\\. Other provisions as to Ministers .- (1) The Prime Minister shall be\n'
  'appointed by the President and the other Ministers shall be appointed by '
  'the\n'
  'President on the advice of the Prime Minister.\n'
  '\n'
  '3[(1A) The total number of Ministers, including the Prime Minister, in the\n'
  'Council of Ministers shall not exceed fifteen per cent. of the total number '
  'of\n'
  'members of the House of the People.\n'
  '\n'
  '(1B) A member of either House of Parliament belonging to any political\n'
  'party who is disqualified for being a member of that House under paragraph '
  '2 of\n'
  'the Tenth Schedule shall also be disqualified to be appointed as a Minister '
  'under\n'
  'clause (1) for duration of the period commencing from the date of his\n'
  'disqualification till the date on which the term of his office as such '
  'member\n'
  'would expire or where he contests any election to either House of '
  'Parliament\n'
  'before the expiry of such period, till the date on which he is declared '
  'elected,\n'
  'whichever is earlier.]\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) The Ministers shall hold office during the pleasure of the President.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) The Council of Ministers shall be collectively responsible to the '
  'House\n'
  'of the People.\n'
  '\n'
  '(4) Before a Minister enters upon his office, the President shall '
  'administer\n'
  'to him the oaths of office and of secrecy according to the forms set out '
  'for the\n'
  'purpose in the Third Schedule.\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Subs. by the Constitution (Forty-second Amendment) Act, 1976, s.13, '
  'for cl. (1)\n'
  '(w.e.f. 3-1-1977).\n'
  '\n'
  '2\\. Ins. by the Constitution (Forty-fourth Amendment) Act, 1978, s. 11 '
  '(w.e.f. 20-6-1979).\n'
  '\n'
  '3\\. Ins. by the Constitution (Ninety-first Amendment) Act, 2003, s. 2 '
  '(w.e.f. 1-1-2004).\n'
