  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '(Part XXI .- Temporary, Transitional and Special Provisions)\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) identification of posts or classes of posts under the State\n'
  'Government and in any body or organisation under the control of the\n'
  'State Government in the Hyderabad-Karnataka region and reservation of\n'
  'a proportion of such posts for persons who belong to that region by birth\n'
  'or by domicile and for appointment thereto by direct recruitment or by\n'
  'promotion or in any other manner as may be specified in the order.]\n'
  '\n'
  '372\\. Continuance in force of existing laws and their adaptation .- (1)\n'
  'Notwithstanding the repeal by this Constitution of the enactments referred '
  'to in\n'
  'article 395 but subject to the other provisions of this Constitution, all '
  'the law in\n'
  'force in the territory of India immediately before the commencement of '
  'this\n'
  'Constitution shall continue in force therein until altered or repealed or '
  'amended\n'
  'by a competent Legislature or other competent authority.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) For the purpose of bringing the provisions of any law in force in the\n'
  'territory of India into accord with the provisions of this Constitution, '
  'the\n'
  'President may by order* make such adaptations and modifications of such '
  'law,\n'
  'whether by way of repeal or amendment, as may be necessary or expedient, '
  'and\n'
  'provide that the law shall, as from such date as may be specified in the '
  'order,\n'
  'have effect subject to the adaptations and modifications so made, and any '
  'such\n'
  'adaptation or modification shall not be questioned in any court of law.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) Nothing in clause (2) shall be deemed-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) to empower the President to make any adaptation or\n'
  'modification of any law after the expiration of 1[three years] from the\n'
  'commencement of this Constitution; or\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) to prevent any competent Legislature or other competent\n'
  'authority from repealing or amending any law adapted or modified by\n'
  'the President under the said clause.\n'
  '\n'

  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '(Part XXI .- Temporary, Transitional and Special Provisions)\n'
  '\n'
  'Explanation I .- The expression "law in force" in this article shall\n'
  'include a law passed or made by a Legislature or other competent authority '
  'in\n'
  'the territory of India before the commencement of this Constitution and '
  'not\n'
  'previously repealed, notwithstanding that it or parts of it may not be then '
  'in\n'
  'operation either at all or in particular areas.\n'
  '\n'
  'Explanation II .- Any law passed or made by a Legislature or other\n'
  'competent authority in the territory of India which immediately before the\n'
  'commencement of this Constitution had extra-territorial effect as well as '
  'effect\n'
  'in the territory of India shall, subject to any such adaptations and '
  'modifications\n'
  'as aforesaid, continue to have such extra-territorial effect.\n'
  '\n'
  'Explanation III .- Nothing in this article shall be construed as '
  'continuing\n'
  'any temporary law in force beyond the date fixed for its expiration or the '
  'date\n'
  'on which it would have expired if this Constitution had not come into '
  'force.\n'
  '\n'
  'Explanation IV .- An Ordinance promulgated by the Governor of a\n'
  'Province under section 88 of the Government of India Act, 1935, and in '
  'force\n'
  'immediately before the commencement of this Constitution shall, unless\n'
  'withdrawn by the Governor of the corresponding State earlier, cease to '
  'operate\n'
  'at the expiration of six weeks from the first meeting after such '
  'commencement\n'
  'of the Legislative Assembly of that State functioning under clause (1) of '
  'article\n'
  '382, and nothing in this article shall be construed as continuing any such\n'
  'Ordinance in force beyond the said period.\n'
  '\n'

  'of bringing the provisions of any law in force in India or in any part '
  'thereof,\n',

  '\n'

  'omitted;\n'
  '\n'
  '(c) in sub-paragraph (2), for clause (d), the following clause shall be\n'
  'substituted, namely :-\n'
  '\n'

  'trade, whether wholesale or retail, except under a licence issued in that '
  'behalf\n'
  'by the District Council:".\n'

  '\n'
  '## PART II CITIZENSHIP\n'
  '\n'
  '5\\. Citizenship at the commencement of the Constitution .- At the\n'
  'commencement of this Constitution, every person who has his domicile in '
  'the\n'
  'territory of India and-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) who was born in the territory of India; or\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) either of whose parents was born in the territory of India; or\n'
  '\n'
  '(c) who has been ordinarily resident in the territory of India for\n'
  'not less than five years immediately preceding such commencement,\n'
  'shall be a citizen of India.\n'
  '\n'
  '6\\. Rights of citizenship of certain persons who have migrated to\n'
  'India from Pakistan .- Notwithstanding anything in article 5, a person who\n'
  'has migrated to the territory of India from the territory now included in\n'
  'Pakistan shall be deemed to be a citizen of India at the commencement of '
  'this\n'
  'Constitution if-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) he or either of his parents or any of his grand-parents was born\n'
  'in India as defined in the Government of India Act, 1935 (as originally\n'
  'enacted); and\n'
  '\n'
  '(b)(i) in the case where such person has so migrated before the\n'
  'nineteenth day of July, 1948, he has been ordinarily resident in the\n'
  'territory of India since the date of his migration, or\n'
  '\n'
  '(ii) in the case where such person has so migrated on or after the\n'
  'nineteenth day of July, 1948, he has been registered as a citizen of India\n'
  'by an officer appointed in that behalf by the Government of the\n'
  'Dominion of India on an application made by him therefor to such\n'
  'officer before the commencement of this Constitution in the form and\n'
  'manner prescribed by that Government:\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that no person shall be so registered unless he has been resident\n'
  'in the territory of India for at least six months immediately preceding the '
  'date\n'
  'of his application.\n'
  '\n'
  '7\\. Rights of citizenship of certain migrants to Pakistan .-\n'
  'Notwithstanding anything in articles 5 and 6, a person who has after the '
  'first\n'
  'day of March, 1947, migrated from the territory of India to the territory '
  'now\n'
  'included in Pakistan shall not be deemed to be a citizen of India:\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="4" -->\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="5" -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '### (Part II .- Citizenship)\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that nothing in this article shall apply to a person who, after\n'
  'having so migrated to the territory now included in Pakistan, has returned '
  'to the\n'
  'territory of India under a permit for resettlement or permanent return '
  'issued by\n'
  'or under the authority of any law and every such person shall for the '
  'purposes\n'
  'of clause (b) of article 6 be deemed to have migrated to the territory of '
  'India\n'
  'after the nineteenth day of July, 1948.\n'
  '\n'
  '8\\. Rights of citizenship of certain persons of Indian origin residing\n'
  'outside India .- Notwithstanding anything in article 5, any person who or\n'
  'either of whose parents or any of whose grand-parents was born in India as\n'
  'defined in the Government of India Act, 1935 (as originally enacted), and '
  'who\n'
  'is ordinarily residing in any country outside India as so defined shall be '
  'deemed\n'
  'to be a citizen of India if he has been registered as a citizen of India by '
  'the\n'
  'diplomatic or consular representative of India in the country where he is '
  'for the\n'
  'time being residing on an application made by him therefor to such '
  'diplomatic\n'
  'or consular representative, whether before or after the commencement of '
  'this\n'
  'Constitution, in the form and manner prescribed by the Government of the\n'
  'Dominion of India or the Government of India.\n'
  '\n'
  '9\\. Persons voluntarily acquiring citizenship of a foreign State not to\n'
  'be citizens .- No person shall be a citizen of India by virtue of article '
  '5, or be\n'
  'deemed to be a citizen of India by virtue of article 6 or article 8, if he '
  'has\n'
  'voluntarily acquired the citizenship of any foreign State.\n'
  '\n'
  '10\\. Continuance of the rights of citizenship .- Every person who is or\n'
  'is deemed to be a citizen of India under any of the foregoing provisions of '
  'this\n'
  'Part shall, subject to the provisions of any law that may be made by '
  'Parliament,\n'
  'continue to be such citizen.\n'
  '\n'
  '11\\. Parliament to regulate the right of citizenship by law .- Nothing\n'
  'in the foregoing provisions of this Part shall derogate from the power of\n'
  'Parliament to make any provision with respect to the acquisition and\n'
  'termination of citizenship and all other matters relating to citizenship.\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## PART III FUNDAMENTAL RIGHTS\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '### General\n'
  '\n'
  '12\\. Definition .- In this Part, unless the context otherwise requires, '
  '"the\n'
  'State" includes the Government and Parliament of India and the Government\n'
  'and the Legislature of each of the States and all local or other '
  'authorities within\n'
  'the territory of India or under the control of the Government of India.\n'
  '\n'
  '13\\. Laws inconsistent with or in derogation of the fundamental\n'
  'rights .- (1) All laws in force in the territory of India immediately '
  'before the\n'
  'commencement of this Constitution, in so far as they are inconsistent with '
  'the\n'
  'provisions of this Part, shall, to the extent of such inconsistency, be '
  'void.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) The State shall not make any law which takes away or abridges the\n'
  'rights conferred by this Part and any law made in contravention of this '
  'clause\n'
  'shall, to the extent of the contravention, be void.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) In this article, unless the context otherwise requires,-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) "law" includes any Ordinance, order, bye-law, rule, regulation,\n'
  'notification, custom or usage having in the territory of India the force '
  'of\n'
  'law;\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) "laws in force" includes laws passed or made by a Legislature\n'
  'or other competent authority in the territory of India before the\n'
  'commencement of this Constitution and not previously repealed,\n'
  'notwithstanding that any such law or any part thereof may not be then in\n'
  'operation either at all or in particular areas.\n'
  '\n'
  '1[(4) Nothing in this article shall apply to any amendment of this\n'
  'Constitution made under article 368.]\n'
  '\n'
  'Right to Equality\n'
  '\n'
  '14\\. Equality before law .- The State shall not deny to any person\n'
  'equality before the law or the equal protection of the laws within the '
  'territory of\n'
  'India.\n'
  '\n'
  '15\\. Prohibition of discrimination on grounds of religion, race, caste,\n'
  'sex or place of birth .- (1) The State shall not discriminate against any '
  'citizen\n'
  'on grounds only of religion, race, caste, sex, place of birth or any of '
  'them.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) No citizen shall, on grounds only of religion, race, caste, sex, place '
  'of\n'
  'birth or any of them, be subject to any disability, liability, restriction '
  'or\n'
  'condition with regard to-\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Ins. by the Constitution (Twenty-fourth Amendment) Act, 1971, s. 2 '
  '(w.e.f. 5-11-1971).\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="6" -->\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="7" -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '### (Part III .- Fundamental Rights)\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) access to shops, public restaurants, hotels and places of public\n'
  'entertainment; or\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) the use of wells, tanks, bathing ghats, roads and places of\n'
  'public resort maintained wholly or partly out of State funds or dedicated\n'
  'to the use of the general public.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) Nothing in this article shall prevent the State from making any\n'
  'special provision for women and children.\n'
  '\n'
  '1[(4) Nothing in this article or in clause (2) of article 29 shall prevent '
  'the\n'
  'State from making any special provision for the advancement of any '
  'socially\n'
  'and educationally backward classes of citizens or for the Scheduled Castes '
  'and\n'
  'the Scheduled Tribes.]\n'
  '\n'
  '2[(5) Nothing in this article or in sub-clause (g) of clause (1) of article '
  '19\n',

  '## PREFACE\n'
  '\n'
  'This is the sixth pocket size edition of the Constitution of\n'
  'India in the diglot form. In this edition, the text of the\n'
  'Constitution of India has been brought up-to-date by\n'
  'incorporating therein all the amendments up to the Constitution\n'
  '(One Hundred and Sixth Amendment) Act, 2023. The foot notes\n'
  'below the text indicate the Constitution Amendment Acts by\n'
  'which such amendments have been made.\n'
  '\n'
  'The Constitution (One Hundredth Amendment) Act, 2015\n'
  'containing details of acquired and transferred territories\n'
  'between the Governments of India and Bangladesh has been\n'
  'provided in Appendix I.\n'
  '\n'
  'The Constitution (Application to Jammu and Kashmir)\n'
  'Order, 2019 and the declaration under article 370(3) of the\n'
  'Constitution have been provided respectively in Appendix II and\n'
  'Appendix III for reference.\n'

  "70\\. Discharge of President's functions in other contingencies .-\n"
  'Parliament may make such provision as it thinks fit for the discharge of '
  'the\n'
  'functions of the President in any contingency not provided for in this '
  'Chapter.\n'
  '\n'
  '1[71. Matters relating to, or connected with, the election of a\n'
  'President or Vice-President .- (1) All doubts and disputes arising out of '
  'or in\n'
  'connection with the election of a President or Vice-President shall be '
  'inquired\n'
  'into and decided by the Supreme Court whose decision shall be final.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) If the election of a person as President or Vice-President is declared\n'
  'void by the Supreme Court, acts done by him in the exercise and '
  'performance\n'
  'of the powers and duties of the office of President or Vice-President, as '
  'the\n'
  'case may be, on or before the date of the decision of the Supreme Court '
  'shall\n'
  'not be invalidated by reason of that declaration.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) Subject to the provisions of this Constitution, Parliament may by law\n'
  'regulate any matter relating to or connected with the election of a '
  'President or\n'
  'Vice-President.\n'
  '\n'
  '(4) The election of a person as President or Vice-President shall not be\n'
  'called in question on the ground of the existence of any vacancy for '
  'whatever\n'
  'reason among the members of the electoral college electing him.]\n'
  '\n'
  '72\\. Power of President to grant pardons, etc., and to suspend, remit\n'
  'or commute sentences in certain cases .- (1) The President shall have the\n'
  'power to grant pardons, reprieves, respites or remissions of punishment or '
  'to\n'
  'suspend, remit or commute the sentence of any person convicted of any\n'
  'offence-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) in all cases where the punishment or sentence is by a Court\n'
  'Martial;\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Subs. by the Constitution (Thirty-ninth Amendment) Act, 1975, s. 2 '
  '(w.e.f 10-8-1975) and\n'
  'further subs. by the Constitution (Forty-fourth Amendment) Act, 1978, s. '
  '10.\n'
  '(w.e.f. 20-6-1979).\n'

  '\n'
  '(Part V .- The Union)\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) in all cases where the punishment or sentence is for an offence\n'
  'against any law relating to a matter to which the executive power of the\n'
  'Union extends;\n'
  '\n'
  '(c) in all cases where the sentence is a sentence of death.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) Nothing in sub-clause (a) of clause (1) shall affect the power\n'
  'conferred by law on any officer of the Armed Forces of the Union to '
  'suspend,\n'
  'remit or commute a sentence passed by a Court Martial.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) Nothing in sub-clause (c) of clause (1) shall affect the power to\n'
  'suspend, remit or commute a sentence of death exercisable by the Governor 1 '
  '***\n'
  'of a State under any law for the time being in force.\n'
  '\n'
  '73\\. Extent of executive power of the Union .- (1) Subject to the\n'
  'provisions of this Constitution, the executive power of the Union shall '
  'extend\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) to the matters with respect to which Parliament has power to make\n'
  'laws; and\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) to the exercise of such rights, authority and jurisdiction as are\n'
  'exercisable by the Government of India by virtue of any treaty or\n'
  'agreement:\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that the executive power referred to in sub-clause (a) shall not,\n'
  'save as expressly provided in this Constitution or in any law made by '
  'Parliament,\n'
  'extend in any State 2 *** to matters with respect to which the Legislature '
  'of the\n'
  'State has also power to make laws.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) Until otherwise provided by Parliament, a State and any officer or\n'
  'authority of a State may, notwithstanding anything in this article, '
  'continue to\n'
  'exercise in matters with respect to which Parliament has power to make laws '
  'for\n'
  'that State such executive power or functions as the State or officer or '
  'authority\n'
  'thereof could exercise immediately before the commencement of this\n'
  'Constitution.\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. The words "or Rajpramukh" omitted by the Constitution (Seventh '
  'Amendment) Act,\n'
  '1956, s. 29 and Sch. (w.e.f. 1-11-1956).\n'
  '\n'
  '2\\. The words and letters "specified in Part A or Part B of the First '
  'Schedule" omitted by\n'
  'the Constitution (Seventh Amendment) Act, 1956, s. 29 and Sch. (w.e.f. '
  '1-11-1956).\n'

  'shall act\n'

  '\n'
  '(2) The question whether any, and if so what, advice was tendered by\n'
  'Ministers to the President shall not be inquired into in any court.\n'
  '\n'
  '75\\. Other provisions as to Ministers .- (1) The Prime Minister shall be\n'
  'appointed by the President and the other Ministers shall be appointed by '
  'the\n'
  'President on the advice of the Prime Minister.\n'
  '\n'
  '3[(1A) The total number of Ministers, including the Prime Minister, in the\n'
  'Council of Ministers shall not exceed fifteen per cent. of the total number '
  'of\n'

  '(1B) A member of either House of Parliament belonging to any political\n'
  'party who is disqualified for being a member of that House under paragraph '
  '2 of\n'
  'the Tenth Schedule shall also be disqualified to be appointed as a Minister '
  'under\n'
  'clause (1) for duration of the period commencing from the date of his\n'

  'Parliament\n'

  'elected,\n'

  'House\n'

  'administer\n'

  '\n'
  '(Part V .- The Union)\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that, where the Court hearing an appeal under any of the\n'
  'provisions of this Chapter other than article 132 consists of less than '
  'five\n'
  'Judges and in the course of the hearing of the appeal the Court is '
  'satisfied that\n'
  'the appeal involves a substantial question of law as to the interpretation '
  'of this\n'
  'Constitution the determination of which is necessary for the disposal of '
  'the\n'
  'appeal, such Court shall refer the question for opinion to a Court '
  'constituted as\n'
  'required by this clause for the purpose of deciding any case involving such '
  'a\n'
  'question and shall on receipt of the opinion dispose of the appeal in '
  'conformity\n'
  'with such opinion.\n'
  '\n'
  '(4) No judgment shall be delivered by the Supreme Court save in open\n'
  'Court, and no report shall be made under article 143 save in accordance '
  'with an\n'
  'opinion also delivered in open Court.\n'
  '\n'
  '(5) No judgment and no such opinion shall be delivered by the Supreme\n'
  'Court save with the concurrence of a majority of the Judges present at the\n'
  'hearing of the case, but nothing in this clause shall be deemed to prevent '
  'a\n'
  'Judge who does not concur from delivering a dissenting judgment or '
  'opinion.\n'
  '\n'
  '146\\. Officers and servants and the expenses of the Supreme Court .-\n'
  '(1) Appointments of officers and servants of the Supreme Court shall be '
  'made\n'
  'by the Chief Justice of India or such other Judge or officer of the Court '
  'as he\n'
  'may direct:\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that the President may by rule require that in such cases as may\n'
  'be specified in the rule, no person not already attached to the Court shall '
  'be\n'
  'appointed to any office connected with the Court, save after consultation '
  'with\n'
  'the Union Public Service Commission.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) Subject to the provisions of any law made by Parliament, the\n'
  'conditions of service of officers and servants of the Supreme Court shall '
  'be\n'
  'such as may be prescribed by rules made by the Chief Justice of India or '
  'by\n'
  'some other Judge or officer of the Court authorised by the Chief Justice '
  'of\n'
  'India to make rules for the purpose:\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that the rules made under this clause shall, so far as they '
  'relate\n'
  'to salaries, allowances, leave or pensions, require the approval of the '
  'President.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) The administrative expenses of the Supreme Court, including all\n'
  'salaries, allowances and pensions payable to or in respect of the officers '
  'and\n'
  'servants of the Court, shall be charged upon the Consolidated Fund of '
  'India,\n'
  'and any fees or other moneys taken by the Court shall form part of that '
  'Fund.\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="68" -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '# THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '(Part V .- The Union)\n'
  '\n'
  '147\\. Interpretation .- In this Chapter and in Chapter V of Part VI,\n'
  'references to any substantial question of law as to the interpretation of '
  'this\n'
  'Constitution shall be construed as including references to any substantial\n'
  'question of law as to the interpretation of the Government of India Act, '
  '1935\n'
  '(including any enactment amending or supplementing that Act), or of any\n'
  'Order in Council or order made thereunder, or of the Indian Independence\n'
  'Act, 1947, or of any order made thereunder.\n'
  '\n'
  'CHAPTER V .- COMPTROLLER AND AUDITOR-GENERAL OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '148\\. Comptroller and Auditor-General of India .- (1) There shall be a\n'
  'Comptroller and Auditor-General of India who shall be appointed by the\n'
  'President by warrant under his hand and seal and shall only be removed '
  'from\n'
  'office in like manner and on the like grounds as a Judge of the Supreme '
  'Court.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) Every person appointed to be the Comptroller and Auditor-General\n'
  'of India shall, before he enters upon his office, make and subscribe before '
  'the\n'
  'President, or some person appointed in that behalf by him, an oath or\n'
  'affirmation according to the form set out for the purpose in the Third '
  'Schedule.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) The salary and other conditions of service of the Comptroller and\n'
  'Auditor-General shall be such as may be determined by Parliament by law '
  'and,\n'
  'until they are so determined, shall be as specified in the Second '
  'Schedule:\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that neither the salary of a Comptroller and Auditor-General\n'
  'nor his rights in respect of leave of absence, pension or age of retirement '
  'shall\n'
  'be varied to his disadvantage after his appointment.\n'
  '\n'
  '(4) The Comptroller and Auditor-General shall not be eligible for further\n'
  'office either under the Government of India or under the Government of any\n'
  'State after he has ceased to hold his office.\n'
  '\n'
  '(5) Subject to the provisions of this Constitution and of any law made by\n'
  'Parliament, the conditions of service of persons serving in the Indian '
  'Audit and\n'
  'Accounts Department and the administrative powers of the Comptroller and\n'
  'Auditor-General shall be such as may be prescribed by rules made by the\n'
  'President after consultation with the Comptroller and Auditor-General.\n'
  '\n'
  '(6) The administrative expenses of the office of the Comptroller and\n'
  'Auditor-General, including all salaries, allowances and pensions payable to '
  'or\n'
  'in respect of persons serving in that office, shall be charged upon the\n'
  'Consolidated Fund of India.\n'
  '\n'

  'The Comptroller and Auditor-General shall perform such duties and exercise\n'
  'such powers in relation to the accounts of the Union and of the States and '
  'of\n',
  'clause (3) as to the measures to be taken for the protection of any '
  'railway, costs\n'
  'have been incurred in excess of those which would have been incurred in '
  'the\n'
  'discharge of the normal duties of the State if such direction had not been '
  'given,\n'
  'there shall be paid by the Government of India to the State such sum as may '
  'be\n'
  'agreed, or, in default of agreement, as may be determined by an arbitrator\n'
  'appointed by the Chief Justice of India, in respect of the extra costs so '
  'incurred\n'
  'by the State.\n'

  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '(Part XI .- Relations between the Union and the States)\n'
  '\n'
  '1[257A. [Assistance to States by deployment of armed forces or other\n'

  'Amendment) Act, 1978, s. 33 (w.e.f. 20-6-1979).]\n'
  '\n'
  '258\\. Power of the Union to confer powers, etc., on States in certain\n'
  'cases .- (1) Notwithstanding anything in this Constitution, the President '
  'may,\n'
  'with the consent of the Government of a State, entrust either conditionally '
  'or\n'
  'unconditionally to that Government or to its officers functions in relation '
  'to any\n'
  'matter to which the executive power of the Union extends.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) A law made by Parliament which applies in any State may,\n'
  'notwithstanding that it relates to a matter with respect to which the '
  'Legislature\n'
  'of the State has no power to make laws, confer powers and impose duties, '
  'or\n'
  'authorise the conferring of powers and the imposition of duties, upon the '
  'State\n'
  'or officers and authorities thereof.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) Where by virtue of this article powers and duties have been conferred\n'
  'or imposed upon a State or officers or authorities thereof, there shall be '
  'paid by\n'
  'the Government of India to the State such sum as may be agreed, or, in '
  'default\n'
  'of agreement, as may be determined by an arbitrator appointed by the Chief\n'
  'Justice of India, in respect of any extra costs of administration incurred '
  'by the\n'
  'State in connection with the exercise of those powers and duties.\n'
  '\n'
  '2[258A. Power of the States to entrust functions to the Union .-\n'
  'Notwithstanding anything in this Constitution, the Governor of a State '
  'may,\n'
  'with the consent of the Government of India, entrust either conditionally '
  'or\n'
  'unconditionally to that Government or to its officers functions in relation '
  'to any\n'
  'matter to which the executive power of the State extends.]\n'
  '\n'
  '[259. Armed Forces in States in Part B of the First Schedule.] .-\n'
  'Omitted by the Constitution (Seventh Amendment) Act, 1956, s. 29 and Sch.\n'
  '(w.e.f. 1-11-1956).\n'
  '\n'
  '260\\. Jurisdiction of the Union in relation to territories outside\n'
  'India .- The Government of India may by agreement with the Government of\n'
  'any territory not being part of the territory of India undertake any '
  'executive,\n'
  'legislative or judicial functions vested in the Government of such '
  'territory, but\n'
  'every such agreement shall be subject to, and governed by, any law relating '
  'to\n'
  'the exercise of foreign jurisdiction for the time being in force.\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Ins. by the Constitution (Forty-second Amendment) Act, 1976, s. 43 '

  '\n'

  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '(Part XI .- Relations between the Union and the States)\n'
  '\n'
  '261\\. Public acts, records and judicial proceedings .- (1) Full faith and\n'
  'credit shall be given throughout the territory of India to public acts, '
  'records and\n'
  'judicial proceedings of the Union and of every State.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) The manner in which and the conditions under which the acts,\n'
  'records and proceedings referred to in clause (1) shall be proved and the '
  'effect\n'
  'thereof determined shall be as provided by law made by Parliament.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) Final judgments or orders delivered or passed by civil courts in any\n'
  'part of the territory of India shall be capable of execution anywhere '
  'within that\n'
  'territory according to law.\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## Disputes relating to Waters\n'
  '\n'
  '262\\. Adjudication of disputes relating to waters of inter-State rivers\n'
  'or river valleys. (1) Parliament may by law provide for the adjudication '
  'of\n'
  'any dispute or complaint with respect to the use, distribution or control '
  'of the\n'
  'waters of, or in, any inter-State river or river valley.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) Notwithstanding anything in this Constitution, Parliament may by\n'
  'law provide that neither the Supreme Court nor any other court shall '
  'exercise\n'
  'jurisdiction in respect of any such dispute or complaint as is referred to '
  'in\n'
  'clause (1).\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## Co-ordination between States\n'
  '\n'
  '263\\. Provisions with respect to an inter-State Council .- If at any time\n'
  'it appears to the President that the public interests would be served by '
  'the\n'
  'establishment of a Council charged with the duty of-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) inquiring into and advising upon disputes which may have\n'
  'arisen between States;\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) investigating and discussing subjects in which some or all of\n'
  'the States, or the Union and one or more of the States, have a common\n'
  'interest; or\n'
  '\n'
  '(c) making recommendations upon any such subject and, in\n'
  'particular, recommendations for the better co-ordination of policy and\n'
  'action with respect to that subject,\n'
  '\n'
  'it shall be lawful for the President by order to establish such a Council, '
  'and to\n'
  'define the nature of the duties to be performed by it and its organisation '
  'and\n'
  'procedure.\n'
  '\n'

  '\n'
  '265\\. Taxes not to be imposed save by authority of law .- No tax shall\n'
  'be levied or collected except by authority of law.\n'
  '\n'
  '266\\. Consolidated Funds and public accounts of India and of the\n'
  'States .- (1) Subject to the provisions of article 267 and to the '

  'net\n'

  'treasury bills, loans or ways and means advances and all moneys received '
  'by\n'
  'that Government in repayment of loans shall form one consolidated fund to '
  'be\n'
  'entitled "the Consolidated Fund of India", and all revenues received by '
  'the\n'
  'Government of a State, all loans raised by that Government by the issue of\n'
  'treasury bills, loans or ways and means advances and all moneys received '
  'by\n'
  'that Government in repayment of loans shall form one consolidated fund to '
  'be\n'
  'entitled "the Consolidated Fund of the State".\n'
  '\n'

  'of India or the Government of a State shall be credited to the public '
  'account of\n'
  'India or the public account of the State, as the case may be.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) No moneys out of the Consolidated Fund of India or the\n'
  'Consolidated Fund of a State shall be appropriated except in accordance '
  'with\n'
  'law and for the purposes and in the manner provided in this Constitution.\n'
  '\n'

  'purposes of meeting unforeseen expenditure pending authorisation of such\n'
  'expenditure by Parliament by law under article 115 or article 116.\n'],

  '\n'
  '#### Right against Exploitation\n'
  '\n'
  '23\\. Prohibition of traffic in human beings and forced labour .- (1)\n'
  'Traffic in human beings and begar and other similar forms of forced labour '
  'are\n'
  'prohibited and any contravention of this provision shall be an offence\n'
  'punishable in accordance with law.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) Nothing in this article shall prevent the State from imposing\n'
  'compulsory service for public purposes, and in imposing such service the '
  'State\n'
  'shall not make any discrimination on grounds only of religion, race, caste '
  'or\n'
  'class or any of them.\n'
  '\n'
  '24\\. Prohibition of employment of children in factories, etc .- No child\n'
  'below the age of fourteen years shall be employed to work in any factory '
  'or\n'
  'mine or engaged in any other hazardous employment.\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '##### Right to Freedom of Religion\n'
  '\n'
  '25\\. Freedom of conscience and free profession, practice and\n'
  'propagation of religion .- (1) Subject to public order, morality and health '
  'and\n'
  'to the other provisions of this Part, all persons are equally entitled to '
  'freedom\n'
  'of conscience and the right freely to profess, practice and propagate '
  'religion.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) Nothing in this article shall affect the operation of any existing law '
  'or\n'
  'prevent the State from making any law-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) regulating or restricting any economic, financial, political or\n'
  'other secular activity which may be associated with religious practice;\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) providing for social welfare and reform or the throwing open\n'
  'of Hindu religious institutions of a public character to all classes and\n'
  'sections of Hindus.\n'
  '\n'
  'Explanation I .- The wearing and carrying of kirpans shall be deemed to\n'
  'be included in the profession of the Sikh religion.\n'
  '\n'
  'Explanation II .- In sub-clause (b) of clause (2), the reference to Hindus\n'
  'shall be construed as including a reference to persons professing the Sikh, '
  'Jaina\n'
  'or Buddhist religion, and the reference to Hindu religious institutions '
  'shall be\n'
  'construed accordingly.\n'
  '\n'
  '26\\. Freedom to manage religious affairs .- Subject to public order,\n'
  'morality and health, every religious denomination or any section thereof '
  'shall\n'
  'have the right-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) to establish and maintain institutions for religious and charitable\n'
  'purposes;\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="15" -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '### (Part III .- Fundamental Rights)\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) to manage its own affairs in matters of religion;\n'
  '\n'
  '(c) to own and acquire movable and immovable property; and\n'
  '\n'
  '(d) to administer such property in accordance with law.\n'
  '\n'
  '27\\. Freedom as to payment of taxes for promotion of any particular\n'
  'religion .- No person shall be compelled to pay any taxes, the proceeds of\n'
  'which are specifically appropriated in payment of expenses for the '
  'promotion\n'
  'or maintenance of any particular religion or religious denomination.\n'
  '\n'
  '28\\. Freedom as to attendance at religious instruction or religious\n'
  'worship in certain educational institutions .- (1) No religious '
  'instruction\n'
  'shall be provided in any educational institution wholly maintained out of '
  'State\n'
  'funds.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) Nothing in clause (1) shall apply to an educational institution which\n'
  'is administered by the State but has been established under any endowment '
  'or\n'
  'trust which requires that religious instruction shall be imparted in such\n'
  'institution.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) No person attending any educational institution recognised by the\n'
  'State or receiving aid out of State funds shall be required to take part in '
  'any\n'
  'religious instruction that may be imparted in such institution or to attend '
  'any\n'
  'religious worship that may be conducted in such institution or in any '
  'premises\n'
  'attached thereto unless such person or, if such person is a minor, his '
  'guardian\n'
  'has given his consent thereto.\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '#### Cultural and Educational Rights\n'
  '\n'
  '29\\. Protection of interests of minorities .- (1) Any section of the\n'
  'citizens residing in the territory of India or any part thereof having a '
  'distinct\n'
  'language, script or culture of its own shall have the right to conserve the '
  'same.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) No citizen shall be denied admission into any educational institution\n'
  'maintained by the State or receiving aid out of State funds on grounds only '
  'of\n'
  'religion, race, caste, language or any of them.\n'
  '\n'
  '30\\. Right of minorities to establish and administer educational\n'
  'institutions .- (1) All minorities, whether based on religion or language, '
  'shall\n'
  'have the right to establish and administer educational institutions of '
  'their\n'
  'choice.\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="16" -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '### (Part III .- Fundamental Rights)\n'
  '\n'
  '1[(1A) In making any law providing for the compulsory acquisition of\n'
  'any property of an educational institution established and administered by '
  'a\n'
  'minority, referred to in clause (1), the State shall ensure that the amount '
  'fixed\n'
  'by or determined under such law for the acquisition of such property is '
  'such as\n'
  'would not restrict or abrogate the right guaranteed under that clause.]\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) The State shall not, in granting aid to educational institutions,\n'
  'discriminate against any educational institution on the ground that it is '
  'under\n'
  'the management of a minority, whether based on religion or language.\n'

  '\n'
  '3 [Saving of Certain Laws]\n'
  '\n'
  '4[31A. Saving of laws providing for acquisition of estates, etc .-\n'
  '5[(1) Notwithstanding anything contained in article 13, no law providing\n',

  '346\\. Official language for communication between one State and\n'

  '347\\. Special provision relating to language spoken by a section of the\n'

  '### CHAPTER IV .- SPECIAL DIRECTIVES\n'
  '\n'
  '350\\. Language to be used in representations for redress of\n'
  'grievances .- Every person shall be entitled to submit a representation for '
  'the\n'
  'redress of any grievance to any officer or authority of the Union or a '
  'State in\n'
  'any of the languages used in the Union or in the State, as the case may '
  'be.\n'
  '\n'
  '2[350A. Facilities for instruction in mother-tongue at primary\n'
  'stage .- It shall be the endeavour of every State and of every local '
  'authority\n'
  'within the State to provide adequate facilities for instruction in the\n'
  'mother-tongue at the primary stage of education to children belonging to\n'
  'linguistic minority groups; and the President may issue such directions to '
  'any\n'
  'State as he considers necessary or proper for securing the provision of '
  'such\n'
  'facilities.\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. The words "or Rajpramukh" omitted by the Constitution (Seventh '
  'Amendment) Act,\n'
  '1956, s. 29 and Sch. (w.e.f. 1-11-1956).\n'
  '\n'
  '2\\. Arts. 350A and 350B ins. by s.21., ibid. (w.e.f. 1-11-1956).\n'
  '\n'

  '\n'
  '<!-- PageNumber="207" -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '# THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA (Part XVII-LANGUAGE)\n'
  '\n'
  '350B. Special Officer for linguistic minorities .- (1) There shall be a\n'
  'Special Officer for linguistic minorities to be appointed by the '
  'President.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) It shall be the duty of the Special Officer to investigate all matters '
  'relating\n'
  'to the safeguards provided for linguistic minorities under this '
  'Constitution and\n'
  'report to the President upon those matters at such intervals as the '
  'President may\n'
  'direct, and the President shall cause all such reports to be laid before '
  'each House of\n'
  'Parliament, and sent to the Governments of the States concerned.]\n'
  '\n'
  '351\\. Directive for development of the Hindi language .- It shall be the\n'
  'duty of the Union to promote the spread of the Hindi language, to develop '
  'it so\n'
  'that it may serve as a medium of expression for all the elements of the\n'
  'composite culture of India and to secure its enrichment by assimilating '
  'without\n'
  'interfering with its genius, the forms, style and expressions used in '
  'Hindustani\n'
  'and in the other languages of India specified in the Eighth Schedule, and '
  'by\n'
  'drawing, wherever necessary or desirable, for its vocabulary, primarily on\n'
  'Sanskrit and secondarily on other languages.\n'
  '\n'
  '<!-- PageBreak -->\n'
  '\n'

  '## PART XVIII EMERGENCY PROVISIONS\n'
  '\n'
  '352\\. Proclamation of Emergency .- (1) If the President is satisfied that\n'
  'a grave emergency exists whereby the security of India or of any part of '
  'the\n'
  'territory thereof is threatened, whether by war or external aggression or '
  '1[armed\n'
  'rebellion], he may, by Proclamation, make a declaration to that effect '
  '2[in\n'
  'respect of the whole of India or of such part of the territory thereof as '
  'may be\n'
  'specified in the Proclamation.]\n'
  '\n'
  '3[Explanation .- A Proclamation of Emergency declaring that the\n'
  'security of India or any part of the territory thereof is threatened by war '
  'or by\n'
  'external aggression or by armed rebellion may be made before the actual\n'
  'occurrence of war or of any such aggression or rebellion, if the President '
  'is\n'
  'satisfied that there is imminent danger thereof.]\n'
  '\n'
  '4[(2) A Proclamation issued under clause (1) may be varied or revoked\n'
  'by a subsequent Proclamation.\n'
  '\n'
  '(3) The President shall not issue a Proclamation under clause (1) or a\n',
  'substantially true report of any proceedings of either House of Parliament '
  'or the\n'
  'Legislative Assembly, or, as the case may be, either House of the '
  'Legislature,\n'
  'of a State, unless the publication is proved to have been made with '
  'malice:\n'
  '\n'
  'Provided that nothing in this clause shall apply to the publication of any\n'
  'report of the proceedings of a secret sitting of either House of Parliament '
  'or the\n'
  'Legislative Assembly, or, as the case may be, either House of the '
  'Legislature,\n'
  'of a State.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) Clause (1) shall apply in relation to reports or matters broadcast by\n'
  'means of wireless telegraphy as part of any programme or service provided '
  'by\n'
  'means of a broadcasting station as it applies in relation to reports or '
  'matters\n'
  'published in a newspaper.\n'
  '\n'
  'Explanation .- In this article, "newspaper" includes a news agency report\n'
  'containing material for publication in a newspaper.]\n'
  '\n'
  '2[361B. Disqualification for appointment on remunerative political\n'
  'post .- A member of a House belonging to any political party who is\n'
  'disqualified for being a member of the House under paragraph 2 of the '
  'Tenth\n'
  'Schedule shall also be disqualified to hold any remunerative political post '
  'for\n'
  'duration of the period commencing from the date of his disqualification '
  'till the\n'
  'date on which the term of his office as such member would expire or till '
  'the\n'
  'date on which he contests an election to a House and is declared elected,\n'
  'whichever is earlier.\n'
  '\n'
  'Explanation .- For the purposes of this article,-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) the expression "House" has the meaning assigned to it in\n'
  'clause (a) of paragraph 1 of the Tenth Schedule;\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) the expression "remunerative political post" means any office-\n'
  '\n'
  '(i) under the Government of India or the Government of a\n'
  'State where the salary or remuneration for such office is paid\n'
  'out of the public revenue of the Government of India or the\n'
  'Government of the State, as the case may be; or\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Art. 361A ins. by the Constitution (Forty-fourth Amendment) Act, 1978, '
  's. 42\n'
  '(w.e.f. 20-6-1979).\n'
  '\n'
  '2\\. Art. 361B ins. by the Constitution (Ninety-first Amendment) Act, 2003, '
  's. 4\n'
  '(w.e.f. 1-1-2004).\n'
  '\n'

  '<!-- PageNumber="221" -->\n'
  '\n'
  '\n'
  '# THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA (Part XIX .- MISCELLANEOUS)\n'
  '\n'
  '(ii) under a body, whether incorporated or not, which is\n'
  'wholly or partially owned by the Government of India or the\n'
  'Government of State, and the salary or remuneration for such\n'
  'office is paid by such body,\n'
  '\n'
  'except where such salary or remuneration paid is compensatory in nature.]\n'
  '\n'
  '362\\. [Rights and privileges of Rulers of Indian States.] .- Omitted by '

  '\n'
  '363\\. Bar to interference by courts in disputes arising out of certain\n'
  'treaties, agreements, etc .- (1) Notwithstanding anything in this '
  'Constitution\n'
  'but subject to the provisions of article 143, neither the Supreme Court nor '
  'any\n'
  'other court shall have jurisdiction in any dispute arising out of any '
  'provision of\n'
  'a treaty, agreement, covenant, engagement, sanad or other similar '
  'instrument\n'
  'which was entered into or executed before the commencement of this\n'

  'the Dominion of India or any of its predecessor Governments was a party '
  'and\n'
  'which has or has been continued in operation after such commencement, or '
  'in\n'
  'any dispute in respect of any right accruing under or any liability or '
  'obligation\n'
  'arising out of any of the provisions of this Constitution relating to any '
  'such\n'
  'treaty, agreement, covenant, engagement, sanad or other similar '
  'instrument.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) In this article-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) "Indian State" means any territory recognised before the\n'
  'commencement of this Constitution by His Majesty or the Government\n'
  'of the Dominion of India as being such a State; and\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) "Ruler" includes the Prince, Chief or other person recognised\n'
  'before such commencement by His Majesty or the Government of the\n'
  'Dominion of India as the Ruler of any Indian State.\n'
  '\n'
  '1[363A. Recognition granted to Rulers of Indian States to cease and\n'
  'privy purses to be abolished .- Notwithstanding anything in this '
  'Constitution\n'
  'or in any law for the time being in force-\n'
  '\n'

  'Act, 1971, was recognised by the President as the Ruler of an Indian\n'
  'State or any person who, at any time before such commencement, was\n'
  'recognised by the President as the successor of such ruler shall, on and\n'
  'from such commencement, cease to be recognised as such Ruler or the\n'
  'successor of such Ruler;\n'
  '\n'
  '1\\. Art. 363A ins. by the Constitution (Twenty-sixth Amendment) Act, 1971, '
  's. 3\n'
  '(w.e.f. 28-12-1971).\n'

  '\n'
  '(b) on and from the commencement of the Constitution (Twenty-\n'
  'sixth Amendment) Act, 1971, privy purse is abolished and all rights,\n'
  'liabilities and obligations in respect of privy purse are extinguished and\n'
  'accordingly the Ruler or, as the case may be, the successor of such\n'
  'Ruler, referred to in clause (a) or any other person shall not be paid any\n'
  'sum as privy purse.]\n'
  '\n'
  '364\\. Special provisions as to major ports and aerodromes .- (1)\n'
  'Notwithstanding anything in this Constitution, the President may by public\n'
  'notification direct that as from such date as may be specified in the\n'
  'notification-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) any law made by Parliament or by the Legislature of a State\n'
  'shall not apply to any major port or aerodrome or shall apply thereto\n'
  'subject to such exceptions or modifications as may be specified in the\n'
  'notification; or\n'
  '\n'
  '(b) any existing law shall cease to have effect in any major port or\n'
  'aerodrome except as respects things done or omitted to be done before\n'
  'the said date, or shall in its application to such port or aerodrome have\n'
  'effect subject to such exceptions or modifications as may be specified in\n'
  'the notification.\n'
  '\n'
  '(2) In this article-\n'
  '\n'
  '(a) "major port" means a port declared to be a major port by or\n'
  'under any law made by Parliament or any existing law and includes all\n'

  '\n'
  '(b) "aerodrome" means aerodrome as defined for the purposes of\n'
  'the enactments relating to airways, aircraft and air navigation.\n'
  '\n'
  '365\\. Effect of failure to comply with, or to give effect to, directions\n'
  'given by the Union .- Where any State has failed to comply with, or to '
  'give\n'
  'effect to, any directions given in the exercise of the executive power of '
  'the Union\n'
  'under any of the provisions of this Constitution, it shall be lawful for '
  'the\n'
  'President to hold that a situation has arisen in which the Government of '
  'the State\n'
  'cannot be carried on in accordance with the provisions of this '
  'Constitution.\n'
  '\n'
  '366\\. Definitions .- In this Constitution, unless the context otherwise\n'
  'requires, the following expressions have the meanings hereby respectively\n'
  'assigned to them, that is to say-\n'
  '\n'
  '(1) "agricultural income" means agricultural income as defined\n'
  'for the purposes of the enactments relating to Indian income-tax;\n'

  '1988\\) (w.e.f. 16-12-1988) s.2, as under-\n'

  '"(d) prescribe that no person resident in the district shall carry on any\n'

  '\n'
  'Provided that no regulations may be made under this paragraph\n'
  'unless they are passed by a majority of not less than three-fourths of the\n'

  '\n'
